Local News

Zhu Ziqiao Reports on Combat Experience 70

Temporary General Assembly of the Local Association

Driven by Conscience, Not to Show Off Merit

Battling Hunger and Cold, Not Disgracing the Mission

| I Hope So, Everyone Hopes So |

Shanghai Shishi Telegraph Agency Local News: Zhu Ziqiao was commissioned by the Local Association last year to lead various volunteer forces in the war of resistance against Japan. However, most of his troops lacked clothing and food, and fought in hunger and cold, so he withdrew to Shanghai to report to the association and seek relief. Yesterday afternoon at 5 PM, the association convened a special temporary meeting, inviting Zhu to report on his combat experiences. The circumstances at that time are recorded below:

Attendees 71

Yesterday afternoon at 5 PM, members of the association arrived continuously. Attendees included Zhu Ziqiao, Shi Liangcai, Wang Xiaolai, Xu Jiluo, Wen Lantao, Kui Yanfang, Huang Renzhi and more than fifty other people.

Agenda 72

At 6:30 PM, the meeting was convened with the ringing of a bell, chaired by Shi Liangcai. The agenda was as follows: (1) Report of Zhu Ziqiao relaying a telegram from Commander Song Zheyuan, thanking the association for their condolences. (2) Report of a telegram from Commander Sun Dianying, thanking the association for their condolences. (3) Report of letters from the North, detailing recent conditions. (4) Zhu Ziqiao, together with Cha Mianzhong, came to the meeting from Beiping to report on the latest combat situation in the North and the handling of relief efforts. (5) Li Liejun's telegram requesting all efforts to assist anti-Japanese soldiers. (6) Report of a letter from Sun Zheyuan's representative, Sun Longqing, requesting that future donations be sent directly to the Bank of China and the Jin Cheng Bank for collection and remittance, and that the current needs are heavy-duty vehicles and cotton overcoats. (7) Discussion of methods to deal with the relief problem in the North. (8) Report of Li Du's representative Liu Piguang, Ma Zhanshan's representative Wu Huanzhang, and five representatives of returning soldiers from Jilin and Heilongjiang, Song Yunzhang, Liang Detang, Zhao Zhuohua, Zhao Shenyuan, and Zhang Chuyu, who came to the meeting to thank the association, request to be rapidly established a solution. (9) The Shanghai Charity Group's United Relief Association for Northeastern Refugees wrote that 158 women and children from Wang Delin's troops have returned to Shanghai, but only 8 have homes to live in, and the rest will have to stay in Shanghai for a long time, requesting a meeting of various groups to discuss solutions. (10) The Shanghai First Special District Citizens' United Association sent a letter requesting the citizens to encourage and establish a wartime organization (resolved to be turned over to the board of directors for discussion). (11) The Merchant National Salvation Association sent a letter describing the visit of representatives to Yuguan for condolences, and requesting assistance in providing materials for building defensive positions, with an attached list of soldiers killed and wounded (resolved to be included in the relief case).

Combat Experience 73

General Zhu Ziqiao reported on his combat experience, saying that in March of last year, from the standpoint of the people and under the mandate of the association, he automatically went north to work. He is now reporting in order to make the patriotic compatriots of the whole country strive to save the loss of the Northeast and to understand the importance of the Northeast. The local people in the Northeast were extremely delighted to see our group going to help. Especially the various groups in Shanghai, which have transferred their spirit of assisting the Nineteenth Route Army in combat to assisting the Northeast, were especially delightful. If the rear can provide further assistance, the volunteer army, which automatically fights for the survival of the country, will surely show even more fighting spirit. The important tasks of the volunteer army in the past, apart from bloody hand-to-hand combat, are to destroy railways to cut off their supplies, and to cut down utility poles to block their news. In the past year, we have made them suffer countless losses. Although the Japanese army's equipment is sophisticated, if we can persevere, victory will surely belong to us. Our stance is to hold on to the determination that we cannot be puppets, and we cannot be slaves to a fallen nation, and we must resist to the end no matter what. However, those fighting on the front lines have no food, no clothing, and face difficulties in transportation. As a result, the troops fighting on the front lines often go without a full meal for one or two days, and some have not changed their underwear for three months. The dire circumstances cannot be described in full. At the same time, on the relief front, the front lines are very far from the rear. The nearest is also seventy or eighty miles away. Rescuers lack automobiles, so they all use manpower, and it takes five or six people to carry one wounded soldier to the rear. Even if there are cars, there is no gasoline. Wood and hospital beds are also extremely scarce. Cotton quilts and clothing are transported day and night, and those who arrive later sleep on the ground. All kinds of tragic scenes are hard to describe. In short, the relief effort is urgently needed, and I hope that the compatriots in the rear will quickly find a way to avoid leaving wounded soldiers from the front without help. My reason for doing this is purely driven by conscience. Today's report has no purpose of showing off merit. If I am like this, I hope that everyone can be like this, then China's future will have hope.

Relief Measures 74

Chairman Shi Liangcai reported that the previously raised 500,000 yuan had generally achieved its purpose, but the silver industry had only raised one-quarter (50,000 yuan), and requested that those present do their best to find a way. He also said that what the front lines lack most is thermos bottles, which should be procured in large numbers. At the same time, two methods were proposed: (1) encourage Zhang Xueliang to donate some, (2) the football community is very enthusiastic about national affairs, so please initiate a charity match. The first point was resolved to be delayed for the time being, and the second point was immediately prepared by the Progressive Association. Regarding the ninth item on the agenda, it was resolved to reply to the Shanghai Charity Group's United Relief Association for Northeastern Refugees that they could find a way to borrow houses, but for finances, please seek to raise funds separately. The meeting was adjourned at over 8 PM.

Wu Chao-shu Speaks

Impact of Japan's Withdrawal from the League of Nations 81

Must Still Fulfill All Obligations for Two Years

Conflicts May Arise Among Britain, America, and Germany Over the Governing of Islands

According to the Central News Agency, Japan formally announced its withdrawal from the League of Nations the day before yesterday. A Central News Agency reporter paid a special visit to diplomat Wu Chao-shu this morning to inquire about the international impact of Japan's withdrawal. Mr. Wu graciously received the reporter and provided a detailed response as follows:

Manifestation of a Mad Psychology According to Mr. Wu, although Japan announced its withdrawal from the League of Nations the day before yesterday, it cannot officially withdraw until March 27, 1935, according to the League of Nations Covenant. During these two years, Japan must still fulfill all the obligations of a member state of the League of Nations. This is like renting a house in Shanghai, where one must give a month's notice before terminating the lease. Only after a month has passed can the lease be terminated. Japan, angered by the League of Nations' upholding of justice, has withdrawn in an attempt to inflict a minor blow on the League. However, during these two years, Japan will still be bound by international covenants and must fulfill its obligations as a member state. Therefore, Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations is actually harmful and not beneficial. However, Japan, knowing that it is harmful and not beneficial, still announced its withdrawal to vent its momentary anger. From this, we can also see a glimpse of the Japanese people's mad psychology. As for the first impact of Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations, it will be to strengthen the world's opinion that is unfavorable to Japan. The second impact will be the conflict arising from the mandated islands.

Conflict Among Britain, America, Germany, and Japan Japan announced its withdrawal from the League of Nations but still wants to retain the South Pacific mandated islands, which is bound to cause conflict with the League of Nations. Moreover, if Japan wants to retain the South Pacific mandated islands, Britain, America, and Germany all have the possibility of direct conflict with Japan. This is because British Australia is adjacent to the South Pacific mandated islands, and Britain is unwilling to have ambitious Japan govern the South Pacific islands. The United States, due to various military and commercial reasons, will also strongly oppose Japan retaining the South Pacific mandated islands. Germany is the former owner of the South Pacific islands and will certainly request their return, canceling Japan's trusteeship. Therefore, the South Pacific mandated island issue will not only cause conflict between Japan and the League of Nations, but Britain, America, and Germany all have the possibility of direct conflict with Japan. This great global upheaval will be triggered by this.

Ambassador Chiang Will Not Return to His Post Temporarily Regarding the Northeast issue, there is currently no possibility of direct negotiations between China and Japan. As for whether the League of Nations can sanction Japan, it still depends on whether Britain, America, and France have the determination to do so. Currently, the diplomatic focus of China and Japan is in Geneva, and the military focus is along the Great Wall. The ambassador to Japan feels that there is nothing to do, so Ambassador Chiang has decided not to return to his post temporarily.

Madam Soong Ching-ling issued a statement yesterday, saying that recently, various Chinese and Western newspapers have contained inaccurate reports about her personal activities. Merchants and Residents of Nanjing Road

Re-Inspection of Inferior Goods Tomorrow 85

Results to be Published in Newspapers

The Nanjing Road Businessmen's Association and the First District Branch of Citizens, considering that the area under their jurisdiction is the bustling center of Shanghai, should be particularly strict in automatically resisting inferior goods in order to maintain appearances and set an example. Therefore, they have organized an Inferior Goods Inspection Committee to conduct impartial inspections. Those who have truly been cleaned up have been issued joint certification plaques to ensure protection. However, the Association recently felt that the situation in North China was precarious. In addition to striving to solicit donations for national salvation and supporting the front lines, they believed that the fundamental way for merchants and residents to save the country was to resolutely engage in economic severance, which was the most important and effective measure. They were deeply concerned that unscrupulous merchants might still be mixed in with the Association's area, secretly selling inferior goods. Therefore, they decided at a meeting yesterday afternoon to convene the former inspectors again, starting at 10:00 AM tomorrow (the 30th), to set off in groups to conduct inspections. Regardless of whether they have received a plaque or are members, they must be inspected one by one, and the results will be published in advertisements in major Shanghai daily newspapers in order to reward or punish them in terms of reputation and to make it easier for patriotic compatriots to know what to choose when purchasing goods.

Representatives of Wang Delin's Family Members

Thanked Various Agencies Yesterday 86

Hoping to Find Ways to Accommodate Family Members of Various Units

Newborn Child Named "Wu Yang," Containing a Double Meaning

Rosters Created to Await Discussion of Methods by All Sectors

After the family members of General Wang Delin, Commander-in-Chief of the Jilin National Salvation Army, and others arrived in Shanghai, they temporarily stayed at the Shanghai Grand Hotel. Wu Huanzhang and other representatives of the Northeast Armies specifically sought assistance from all sectors yesterday and have created rosters to send to various organizations. The details are recorded separately below.

Expressing Gratitude to All Sectors 87

Song Yunzhang, Zhao Shenyuan, Liang Detang, Zhang Chuyu, and other representatives of the unit, together with personnel from the Shanghai Liaison Office of the Northeast Anti-Japanese Armies, such as Wu Huanzhang, representative of Ma Zhanshan, Liu Piguang, representative of Li Du, Zhao Zhuohua, representative of Feng Zhanhai, and other seven people, visited the Municipal Government, Municipal Public Security Bureau, Local Association, Northeast Association, Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association, various charitable organizations, the United Association for Relief of Northeast Refugees, the Chinese Women's Association for Relief of Northeast Compatriots, and other organizations yesterday to express their gratitude for the enthusiasm of all sectors in caring for the unit's arrival in Shanghai. Public Security Bureau Director Wen Hongen, Local Promotion Association President Shi Liangcai, and others personally received them and expressed their willingness to do their best to help with the aftermath of the unit's family members.

Long-Term Plans Should Be Considered 88

According to Liang Detang, the Shanghai representative of Commander Wang Delin, after the family members of our unit came to Shanghai, they were given food and lodging by various organizations and were warmly received, and the cost of meals and accommodation was paid on their behalf. We are deeply grateful for the thoughtful care. However, we believe that paying around 100 yuan per day for meals and accommodation at a Shanghai hotel is not a long-term plan. In the future, other Northeast Anti-Japanese Armies, such as those of Ma Zhanshan, Su Bingwen, Li Du, and Feng Zhanhai, may continue to send their family members to Shanghai in order to eliminate any worries about the rear. Therefore, in order to seek a once-and-for-all solution, it seems that a more spacious location should be found so that the family members of the anti-Japanese soldiers can have a place to settle down. Then the anti-Japanese soldiers will have no family burden and can concentrate on fighting the enemy for the country. When we went to various agencies and organizations to express our gratitude today, we expressed this intention to all sectors.

Petitioning the Central Government 89

As for this once-and-for-all plan, it seems that it should be organized and handled by the government authorities and supported by local organizations. The care given to the family members of our unit by various sectors this time has already cost a lot, and the mutual assistance between the people has reached its limit. If the Central Government can accommodate the family members of the anti-Japanese soldiers as much as possible, then the soldiers will be able to serve with peace of mind, which is tantamount to encouraging the soldiers, and its effect is equal to providing relief. Therefore, we may unite the representatives of various units stationed in Shanghai and go to Beijing to petition the Central Government.

Child Named Wu Yang 90

Liang also said that after the family members of the unit arrived in Shanghai a few days ago, the boy born to the wife of Adjutant Wang Wujiang within half an hour was named "Wu Yang" after mutual consultation by all the family members. This contains a double meaning: one is to express the safe birth after arriving in Shanghai on the Wu Yang Wheel, and the other is to hope that our four northeastern provinces can return safely and be restored to our country's territory.

Detailed Rosters 91

Detailed rosters of the unit's family members, which were previously requested by the United Association of Charitable Organizations, were created yesterday and sent to the United Association of Organizations for transcription and forwarding to the Local Association to discuss specific methods for settling the unit's family members.

Letter Requesting Discussion 92

The United Association of Charitable Organizations of this city sent a letter to the Local Association yesterday, saying: "Respectfully, we received a previous letter stating that according to the telegram from Liang Yuanshanqiao, representative of Wang Delin, Commander of the National Salvation Army, Wang's unit's military women and children entered Russia and returned to China, and the remaining 158 family members went directly to Shanghai, requesting assistance. Now, the family members have arrived in Shanghai a few days ago and are staying at the Shanghai Tai Hotel in Baoyu Lane, French Concession. According to reports from Chen Wenkui and Ge Yunxun, the staff members sent by our association to receive them, only eight of these family members have homes to return to, and the rest are all from the three northeastern provinces. Their husbands are all on the front lines and must stay in Shanghai for a long time. The daily expenses are huge and difficult to sustain. Accordingly, we are writing to your association to convene a meeting of various organizations to discuss a long-term maintenance plan. We are very hopeful. Sincerely, to the Shanghai Local Association."

Women's Condolences 93

In addition to sending representatives to welcome them at the port, the Chinese Women's Association for Relief of Northeast Compatriots also sent representatives Huang Shaoxiong's wife Cai Fengzhen, Wu Tiecheng's wife Shen Huiru, Ma Chaojun's wife Shen Huilian, Gan Naiguang's wife Chen Xingrong, He Xiangning's representative Zhang Qiong, and Ms. Wei Qiongying and Liang Deyi to express their condolences. The association had originally prepared to provide relief in the form of money and goods, but Madam Wang indicated that those who came to Shanghai this time were only the family members of Wang's unit. During this time of national crisis, they only hoped to be able to live. What they most hoped for was to provide the front lines with shells and food so that they could destroy the enemy. They also said that General Wang would also arrive in Shanghai next month. The meeting decided to provide them with concrete assistance.

Health Bureau

Initiating a Tuberculosis Prevention Association 94

Mayor Wu Supports and Promotes

The health authorities of this city have recently launched a movement to initiate the organization of a Tuberculosis Prevention Association. It is heard that the motivation for this movement came from Dr. Bu Mei, a Cantonese and director of the Department of Cardiology and Pulmonary Medicine at the Red Cross Hospital last year. He noted that the number of citizens in this city suffering from tuberculosis has been increasing year by year, and tuberculosis is easy to spread, and those who suffer from this disease will suffer health damage at minimum and loss of life at worst. The movement was launched so that we must urgently seek preventive measures. Therefore, there was a discussion about organizing a Tuberculosis Prevention Association. Dr. Bu Mei had repeated consultations with Mr. Li Tingan, Director of the Municipal Health Bureau, and Mr. Wu Liande, Director of the Seaport Epidemic Prevention Office. Recently, the draft of the opinion letter has been completed. The content of the opinion letter is divided and described below.

Feng Yuxiang's Letter to Ninety-Four Elder 95

Agrees with the Intolerable Association

Feng Yuxiang, who is rumored to be going to Beijing to jointly face the national crisis, sent a letter to Ninety-Four Elder Ma Xiangbo yesterday, saying: "Elder Ma, I am honored to hear of your well-being. This time, the Japanese army is invading Rehe and planning to disturb North China. If our country does not strive to save itself, the danger of partition and joint administration may come sooner than we expect. Therefore, the way to save the country should be to seek it from the people as the most urgent task at present. The elder initiated the Intolerable Association to advocate for the world, and it will surely awaken the deaf and inspire the foolish, making the cowardly stand up and the timid be brave, restoring the national spirit and a lasting struggle with the Japanese bandits. I am far away in the northern border and cannot help but offer my advance congratulations. I am very impressed that Father Lebbe, as a foreigner, is so enthusiastic and righteous. The front line is tense these days, and rescue work is very important. I will try to do what you and the other gentlemen have hoped for. I am concerned about your health, so I am writing to inform you first. Sincerely, I respectfully wish you blessings and peace. Your student Feng Yuxiang bows."

Promotion Method Before the establishment of the association, it will first publicly solicit members who support this work. People of all nationalities and genders can join the association to promote it universally. The association plans to unite the Shanghai Chinese Medical Association, the Public Health Committee, the Shanghai Public Health Association, and other medical groups to jointly develop epidemic prevention affairs, and to invite well-known groups in this city, such as the Young Men's and Women's Christian Associations, the Orphanage, the Shanghai Race Club, the Youth Society, the Red Cross Society, the Rotary Club, the Health Department of the International League of Nations, and various university clubs, to participate and share the responsibility of prevention.

Soliciting Members In the future, for the matter of soliciting members, it is planned to first appoint Mayor Wu Tiecheng, major philanthropists, leaders of various organizations, famous ladies, and celebrities in the medical field to serve as sponsors and promoters, and then separately solicit members. Members are divided into four groups: (1) Supporting members, who pay an annual membership fee of 100 yuan; (2) Maintaining members, who pay an annual membership fee of 25 yuan; (3) Ordinary members, who pay an annual membership fee of 5 yuan; (4) Junior members, who pay an annual membership fee of 1 yuan.

Page 10

Association Organization After the association is established, there will be one president, who will be Mayor Wu, four vice presidents (two men and two women), one honorary treasurer, and two honorary secretaries (one Chinese and one foreign). Various committees are also planned to be organized: (1) Standing Committee (organized by 30 members); (2) Finance Committee (organized by 10 members); (3) Soliciting Committee (organized by 5 members); (4) Medical Committee (organized by 5 members); (5) Executive Committee (organized by 5 people jointly recommended by the Finance and Medical Committees). The association should have one responsible director and several assistants to carry out the work.

Business Outline The association plans to set up (1) a clinic, (2) a tuberculosis hospital, and (3) a tuberculosis sanatorium, and pay attention to publicity. As for the organization of the various hospitals and sanatoriums, it is still under discussion.

Zhu Jiqing's Telegram 97

Reasons for the Fall of Rehe

Zhu Jiqing, the Director-General of the Northeast National Salvation Army, sent a telegram to a certain Central Committee member in Nanjing from the front line on the 23rd of this month, the original text of which is as follows: (Omitted above) (2) This time, the Japanese army invaded Rehe. The troops in Chaoyang were less than 2,000, and those in Kairu on the left wing and Lingnan on the right wing were also less than 1,000. Even with the puppet army, the total number was less than 20,000. We had hundreds of thousands of troops, but we were defeated in one battle. Rehe was lost in less than ten days. Moreover, the enemy had a thorough understanding of our military situation, but we knew nothing about the enemy's movements. Our actions were slow and our responses were ineffective, while the enemy tried to be swift and took us by surprise. They knew that the people of Rehe had a deep hatred for Tang [Yulin] and used guides. They knew that Shao Benliang had a grudge against the Dong brigade and sought to use them as vanguards. They also used news to exaggerate their propaganda and collected more than 3,000 large vehicles loaded with sandbags and a small number of Japanese troops to bolster their momentum and cover up their intentions. Our army did not notice and was demoralized before the battle. (3) Many officers lacked national consciousness and a sense of the country. In this kind of national war, they still focused on preserving their strength and were accustomed to leisure. Not only did they have no combat plans, but they did not pay attention to the war. For example, when the enemy reached Lingyuan, [name omitted] was still eating peacefully. The 19th Brigade was ordered to change defenses, but before the 1st Brigade that was supposed to take over arrived at the position, they retreated first. The enemy took the opportunity to attack and lost Lingnan. Chaoyang, as the gateway to Rehe, was entrusted to the Rehe army, which was unable to withstand a single blow. (4) In the past, the authorities imposed harsh policies and abused the people, causing widespread resentment. The ignorant people took the opportunity to complain and were willing to be accomplices to the enemy. (5) In peacetime, the army was not paid, and in wartime, the generals did not go to the front. The soldiers had no will to fight, and some even turned against each other. For example, Shao Benliang's attack on Chaoyang was a current fact. (6) All the armies were stationed more than 200 li away from the enemy, abandoning the natural defenses and not defending them, as if there was a predetermined plan to abandon Rehe. I do not know what their hearts and livers are made of. (7) All the armies that resisted the enemy adopted a strategy of only defending and not attacking, leading to a decline in morale. They also did not coordinate and fought separately, causing the enemy to break them individually. The above are the main reasons for the loss of Rehe. The number of invading Japanese troops was not large, and they have been fighting for more than a month, so their casualties should also be considerable. To this day, we have not seen a large number of reinforcements. The enemy's current strength in Rehe is very weak, and the river channels on all roads are about to thaw, and the armored vehicles on which the enemy relies have lost their power. If elite troops with combat experience can be selected, (omitted) then they can be wiped out in one fell swoop. I hope you will consider this carefully. (Omitted below) Zhu Jiqing kowtows.

Twenty Years Later

Three Million Overseas Chinese in Thailand Will Forget Their Ancestral Country 98

Siamese Government Implements Assimilation Policy

Forcing Chinese Children to Study Siamese

Overseas Chinese in Thailand Telegraph the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Negotiate

Recently, due to the weak means of the diplomatic authorities of the motherland, our overseas Chinese compatriots have been subjected to heavy oppression by the local governments of various countries. Japan refuses Chinese people from landing, the British and Dutch colonies in Southeast Asia increase various taxes, and recently the Siamese government, in order to naturalize the three million overseas Chinese in Thailand as Siamese citizens, has formulated various acculturation policies, strictly implemented them, and revised immigration regulations and increased import and export taxes to show restrictions. The overseas Chinese in Thailand have telegraphed the diplomatic authorities, requesting negotiations to stop these measures. The details are recorded separately below.

Changing to Siamese Bookkeeping 99

Our compatriots residing in Siam, according to official statistics from the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, number over three million. They mostly run food stalls and small businesses in various parts of Siam. Because the Siamese government levies extremely heavy taxes, their lives are quite difficult. All the accounting books for incoming and outgoing goods, as well as daily records of business income, must bear stamps issued by the Siamese government. However, the use of Chinese bookkeeping was permitted, and the Siamese government did not restrict it. Recently, however, in order to implement its assimilation plan, the Siamese government has strictly ordered Chinese shops in all locations to uniformly adopt Siamese bookkeeping for their accounts from now on. On the surface, this is said to facilitate inspection, but in reality, it is intended to gradually make overseas Chinese forget the writing of their motherland and to become naturalized Siamese citizens.

Increasing Import and Export Taxes 100

In addition to implementing the above-mentioned insidious plan, the Siamese government has also revised immigration conditions and increased the import tax on Chinese people to show restriction. The import tax for Chinese entering Siam used to be 40 baht, but it has now been increased to 100 baht (approximately equivalent to more than 160 Chinese yuan). Restrictions on Chinese children leaving the country are even stricter. In addition to paying a deposit of 500 baht, they must also submit a Siamese diploma; otherwise, they will not be allowed to leave the country. For adults, the export tax has also increased from 5 baht to 20 baht.

Strictly Ordering the Teaching of Siamese 101

As for schools founded by overseas Chinese in Siam, the position of principal must be filled by a Siamese person appointed by the Siamese government. All subjects are also standardized according to the educational regulations promulgated by the Siamese government, with Siamese as the basic course. Therefore, Siamese must be taught for at least 25 hours per week, while Chinese is only taught for one hour per day. Other languages such as English and Japanese are also considered more important than Chinese. The purpose is none other than to make Chinese children, when they grow up, only know Siamese and not Chinese. The viciousness of its assimilation policy is truly chilling. Overseas Chinese, being in a foreign land, have no way to resist and can only be slaughtered. I fear that in twenty years, these millions of overseas Chinese will no longer be part of our Chinese nation. I deeply hope that the government authorities will immediately find a way to lodge a strong protest with the Siamese government in order to open a lifeline for our overseas Chinese in Siam.

Youth Association

Starting Wartime Service Work 102

Mr. Liang Xiaochu, acting director-general of the Youth Association, went north the week before last to investigate the progress of the war and to solicit opinions from military and political authorities on the Youth Association's wartime service work. The Shanghai Youth Association has purchased six large balloons and other entertainment items to send to the front. It is said that the most needed items at the front are undershirts, dirty pants, socks, and towels for clothing, and preserved plums and beef jerky for food.

Employees Laid Off from Two Railways

Petitioned Party and Government Agencies Yesterday 104

Requesting a Clear Announcement or Reinstatement

Various Agencies Promised to Investigate and Reconsider

Huang Boqiao, director of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, has been trying to reorganize and repay foreign debts since taking office, and has laid off a large number of redundant employees. The laid-off employees sent representatives Cai Xiaoqiang, Chen Bingxuan, Li Rensheng, Mao Yinbai, and four others to the special party headquarters of the two railways, the trade unions of the two railways, the municipal party headquarters, and the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday morning to petition, requesting (1) that all laid-off employees be reinstated, (2) that if old employees cannot be reinstated, no new employees can be hired, and (3) that if laid-off personnel are found to have engaged in fraud or dereliction of duty, the facts should be clearly announced. Nanyang Tobacco Factory Dispute Tried Yesterday 105

Party and Government Agencies Confer

Special District Court Opens Trial

Trade Union Makes Some Clarifications

In the case of the labor-management dispute at the Nanyang Tobacco Factory, the situation has become serious again because Wu Linkun, the legal counsel of the factory, arrested workers. Yesterday, party and government agencies conferred on the steps to mediate, the court tried the detained workers, and the trade union council made important remarks on the Nanyang Tobacco Factory's statement. Details are recorded separately below.

Party and Government Conference The party and government agencies believe that the internal investigation company refuses to withdraw, and even claims that the patrol room automatically sent the arrested workers, and the arrested workers have not been released. In order to resolve the dispute as soon as possible, the Social Affairs Bureau sent Wang Xianqing, director of the mediation section, and the Party Department sent Zhang Sheng, a cadre of the civil training section, to the Social Affairs Bureau to discuss mediation steps.

Court Opens Trial In the labor unrest dispute at the Nanyang Tobacco Factory, Zhang Desheng, the foreman of the tobacco leaf room, took the opportunity to use violent means, carrying weapons and inviting many people to arbitrarily destroy objects in the tin packaging department, and severely beat the staff members Li Zhitang, Li Chengyao, and Chen Ronggui, who worked in the engineering department, and sent them to Baolong Hospital on Baker Road, the Blue Cross Society on Haining Road, and other hospitals for treatment. The Chinese and Western detectives of the Huishan Patrol Room have successively arrested the culprit Zhang Desheng and the accomplices Wu Shiyuan, Li Ajin, Li Gui, and Li Xinfa and others, and sent them to the First Special District Court for interrogation. Yesterday morning, the patrol room sent Zhang and other five people to the Third Criminal Court. The trial judge Xiao Xiefen and the chief prosecutor Wang Zuze attended the trial. The patrol room's lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated that the victims Li Zhitang and Li Chengyao in this case are seriously injured in Baolong Hospital on Baker Road. Wu Linkun, the legal counsel of the company, said that Li Zhitang's condition is critical, his brain is injured, thick blood is flowing out, or it will worsen, and his life is at stake. Therefore, he requested the court to go to the hospital with the prosecutor and the forensic doctor to examine his condition in order to clarify the truth. There are two other victims in this case, one is Zhou Gengsheng, and the other is Xu Shunqing, who are also workers in the factory. They were also affected at the time and were sent to Yueming Guangdong Hospital at No. 469 North Sichuan Road. The injuries are also severe. The patrol room sent people to investigate the hospital. According to the doctor, they need to be treated for two weeks before they can be discharged from the hospital. It is hoped that the court will also send a forensic doctor to examine the injuries of the two people. Because the crowd was chaotic at the time, it was impossible to find out. There are a total of four victims in the hospital in this case. Now only Chen Ronggui, who has recovered, is in court. This case cannot proceed, so please postpone it until all the victims have recovered. Then, lawyer Wu Linkun immediately stated the main points of the victims' injuries, saying that Li Zhitang's right skull was damaged, causing thick blood to flow out, and he was the most severely injured. Li Chengyao suffered head injuries and was in a coma. Zhou Gengsheng's head was swollen and his nose was also injured. Xu Shunqing's brain was injured. All of them were consulted by doctors. The rest of the requests were the same as those of lawyer Zhang from the patrol room. According to Chen Ronggui's testimony, his back and chest injuries have improved slightly, and he is helping in the company's engineering department, but not for long. He could not identify the faces of the defendants, and at that time, everyone was hitting each other with iron wooden sticks, etc. According to Zhang Sheng, a representative of the Municipal Party Department, Wu Shiyuan did come to report at 10:10 a.m. and went to the company with representatives from the Social Affairs Bureau and the General Labor Union to mediate and discuss solutions with lawyer Wu Linkun. When questioned, the defendants all denied participating in the beating of the staff, and hired lawyers Wu Shou Gong, Fan Gang, and Ling Qigan to request bail for trial. Judge Xiao ordered the two defendants Wu Shiyuan and Li Xinfa to pay a bail of 500 yuan each, and the rest were detained and re-examined on another day.

Trade Union's Statement Yesterday, Zhou Xuexiang, the executive director of the Fourth District Cigarette Industry Trade Union, told the reporter of the New Voice News Agency about the company's statement the day before yesterday that many of the contents of the statement published in the newspapers yesterday did not match the facts. He made the following clarifications: (1) The so-called statements made by the labor representatives are not the true intentions of all the workers. Only a very small number of bad elements collude with private individuals, engage in private fraud, fabricate all kinds of rumors, and accuse the company of oppressing workers. The office has submitted the application to the party and government agencies. It is a pure organization of all factory employees. The starting point for making statements is naturally in the name of the office, which is expected by the public. What is the so-called small number of bad elements fabricating rumors? As for the company oppressing workers, secretly reporting to the patrol room to arrest workers, and deploying investigators in the factory, the facts are all there, so there is no need to fabricate them. (2) Whether the company's losses are due to high wages or oppression by the trade union, the company's profits last year were not earned by the Shanghai factory alone, and the profits were due to the joint efforts of all employees. It goes without saying that the previous factory closure was due to the pressure of the trade union and wages. Now that the office has been established, it is feared that it will be detrimental to itself, so it deliberately sabotages it. As for the company's profits last year, it has been explained in the statement that it was the joint effort of all employees, and it cannot be achieved by one person. (3) Now the company has expelled the former chief engineer for embezzling the bonus of all workers after investigation, but the so-called worker representatives demand that the former chief engineer be reinstated. It is not necessary for the workers to advise the company on the appointment and dismissal of staff. Since the former chief engineer has been in office, he has been trying to reorganize the factory and has made outstanding achievements. The company dismissed him because he had not been to the factory for a long time, which is not appropriate. Therefore, it sent a letter to the company requesting it to be recorded. This is an expression of intention. As for the embezzlement of workers' bonuses, it is not known what the intention is. (4) During the strike a few days ago, workers and staff clashed. The patrol room arrested the troublemakers on the spot and sent them to the court for punishment. The witnesses on the scene testified in court to exercise their due rights. After the establishment of the office, it put forward preconditions and requested the company to recognize it. Not only did the company ignore it, but it also secretly instigated traitors to use salary increases and promotions as a slogan to implement means of alienation and sabotage of the workers' organization, which aroused the indignation of all workers and caused a voluntary strike. The director Zhang Desheng advised the workers on the spot to maintain order, and was arrested as a result. The false witnesses in court even falsely accused the director Wu Shiyuan of being one of the murderers. At the time of the strike, Wu Shiyuan was in the Municipal Party Department to discuss important matters. How could he have committed the murder? Whether the witnesses were hired and whether they were true or false can be proven by the Municipal Party Department. (5) The company has never prevented honest workers from joining the trade union, and has given detailed consideration and peaceful answers to the preconditions put forward. The company has never expressed its recognition of the office, that is, it does not prevent workers from joining the trade union, gives detailed consideration to the preconditions, and gives peaceful answers. This is a hypocritical high-sounding statement. (6) The legitimacy of the organization of the office must be inquired first. The office has submitted the application to the party and government agencies for organization and establishment, and the party and government authorities have recognized it as a legitimate organization. There is no need for the company to review whether it is legal or not. (7) It is said that since there was no consultation on the dismissal of the chief engineer by the factory, how could the office be hastily declared established the second day after the dismissal? The establishment of the office was reported to the party and government agencies in advance to send personnel to supervise the election. At this time, how could we know the company's conspiracy to dismiss the chief engineer? The claim that it was intentionally hastily established is self-defeating. As for their request to release the detained workers after the riot, it is also said that the company cannot do anything about it. Since there was no reason to stop the riot on the morning of the 19th, and many people were beaten and objects were destroyed, it should be dealt with according to law. After the strike, the party and government agencies sent people to persuade the workers to resume work. Wu Linkun, the representative of the factory, admitted that the company was responsible and released the innocent people that night. The arrested director Zhang Desheng is now claiming that the company cannot do anything about it. The intention of this kind of insidious deception can be known. The above-mentioned points are the true situation of the process, and the company conceals the facts, spreads fallacies, and confuses the public, which is very unfortunate.

International

Cotton Conference Decided to Stop Work for One Week 107

The Shanghai Chinese Cotton Mill Federation received a telegram from the International Textile Industry Federation saying that the International Cotton Committee held a meeting in Brussels on March 20 and unanimously decided to stop work for one week in April this year for textile mills in various countries that are members of the association in order to make the production of textile mills adapt to the needs. It is reported that there are currently 161.1 million spindles in the world, of which 112 million belong to member countries of the International Cotton Spinning Federation, accounting for 69% of the total world.

Page 11

County Executive Committee

Promote the Meaning of Thrift 110

The Shanghai County Executive Committee has designated yesterday to the 3rd of next month as the Thrift Promotion Week, sending personnel to various districts every day to conduct expanded publicity, and issuing a letter to the public, outlining the important significance of the National Thrift Movement as follows: (1) Thrift is purely a kind of economic salvation movement with positive and striving functions, and it is by no means a passive act of stinginess, but rather actual hoarding. Its purpose is to save extravagance in the economic field, and to value time in the work field, strive to increase production, enrich national strength, and expand the power to resist insults. (3) Our front-line soldiers are currently fighting hard against Japan. The compatriots who live in the rear cannot only express gratitude and respect, but must also fulfill their responsibilities. We must know that we can still live and work in peace today, and avoid the trampling of Japanese bandits, thanks to the soldiers on the front line who endure hunger and hardship. Since we in the rear cannot all go to the front line to help resist the enemy, we should, in addition to being well-fed and clothed, consider the plight of the soldiers on the front line, save all expenses, and continuously provide relief to the hard-fought soldiers who are resisting the enemy, and relieve the compatriots who have suffered in the war zone, in order to express the spirit of sharing the same hatred and fulfilling the responsibility of mutual assistance among compatriots. (3) Thrift can not only save waste, but is also the only effective method of economic severance with Japan. All Japanese goods should be rejected and not purchased. All daily necessities that can be saved should also be saved as much as possible. If there are domestic goods that can be substituted, domestic goods must be used. In this way, the sales of Japanese goods in our country will be cut off, and there will be economic panic in Japan. There is no need to cross the sea to the east to conquer, which is enough to kill Japanese imperialism.

Robbery and Shooting at a Tobacco and Paper Shop on Meizhou Road 112

The Mistress Was Shot and Killed by Thieves 113

Zhenxin Paper and Tobacco Sundries Store, located at No. 313 Meizhou Road, Yangshupu, was opened by Gao Zhengbang, a native of Yangzhou. Gao is 34 years old and married a woman from his hometown, Zhou, who is 31 years old. At about 8 o'clock last night, when the store was about to close, three bandits with Jiangbei accents wearing blue cloth shirts and trousers suddenly came. Two bandits were guarding the door, and one entered the store with a handgun and began to overturn the money counter, hoping to rob the store. Zhou saw the opportunity and took the opportunity to escape from the store and ran into the road, shouting for help to catch the robbers. The robber in the house also rushed out of the store. Because Zhou continued to shout, the robber became anxious and fired three shots. One shot hit Zhou in the waist from behind, and Zhou fell to the ground in response. Neighbors and others rushed to the scene after hearing the alarm, but the robbers had already escaped without a trace. They rushed to search for them. Zhou's husband, Gao Zhengbang, returned home and reported to the Yangshupu Patrol Room. The patrol room immediately sent detectives to the scene to investigate and search everywhere. However, Zhou died on the spot because she was shot in a vital part. The patrol room sent the corpse to the mortuary for examination and reported to the court for an autopsy this morning.

Identified and Arrested by Two Detectives from the Zhejiang Provincial Government

Currently Investigating the Case and Detaining Him for Trial

At 6 p.m. the day before yesterday, two detectives from the Security Department of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, Ying Zhiqiao and Liu Ruibiao, reported to the Laozha Patrol Room that Chen Jixue, a native of Shaoxing, had committed a major crime in Shaoxing City and Yuyao, including kidnapping Cao Zikun's son A Yu and Zhao Yinsheng's son, extorting 70,000 yuan, and killing the family members of Shen Yingxiang, the former manager of the Zhihe Qianzhuang. The chief patrol officer ordered Chinese detective Chen Yonggui and others to go to the address and arrest him. After the arrest, the police immediately reported to the First Special District Court. The criminal court of the court, Qian Hongye, interrogated him. The patrol room's lawyer, Ru Baoyi, stated that the case was serious and the patrol room was conducting a thorough investigation. Therefore, he requested that the request of the Zhejiang Security Department to transfer the case be postponed. He only requested that Chen be detained temporarily. Chen immediately claimed that the two detectives from Zhejiang Province were related to the kidnapping of the vice president of the China-South Bank and Xu Chongzhi's son, and hired lawyer Du Jimei to defend him. Judge Qian said that the patrol room only requested detention for investigation, and the details of the case had not yet been investigated. Therefore, it was not necessary to state the case. City Chamber of Commerce's Letter to the French Municipal Council

Prohibiting Police from Wantonly Prying Off Vehicle Licenses 117

The City Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the French Concession Municipal Council yesterday, which reads: "Respectfully, on the 27th of this month, the City Rickshaw Trade Association reported that member rickshaw dealers have been reporting in recent days that French Concession police officers, regardless of whether the rickshaw licenses are Chinese or French, are wantonly prying them off. Moreover, many police stations have set up counters for rickshaw pullers to pay fines, which resembles a business transaction. Upon investigation, the Municipal Council of the said concession has already issued licenses, and these licenses should be valid for passage in the Chinese areas. If rickshaw pullers violate police regulations, they would willingly accept the consequences. However, the use of brute force is unfair. Furthermore, rickshaw pullers live in extreme hardship. If they are subjected to unwarranted searches, wouldn't they be placed in a desperate situation? Therefore, we hereby petition your council to consider their plight and forward this to the French Concession Municipal Council, instructing the Municipal Council to prohibit acts of violence in order to alleviate the hardships of merchants and save the suffering of laborers." According to this, the police officers in the concession wantonly prying off rickshaw licenses is indeed a common occurrence. However, if rickshaw pullers occasionally violate police regulations, there should be proper procedures for punishment. If they pry off licenses without investigating whether there was a violation, rickshaw pullers will not be able to work and will have to painfully scrape together money to pay the fine. This is contrary to the original intention of issuing licenses. We hereby respectfully request that your esteemed council investigate and instruct the relevant authorities to prohibit such actions, so as to maintain the livelihoods of the laborers. We earnestly hope for your consideration."

Mining and Metallurgical Engineering Society

Annual Meeting to be Held in Hangzhou This Year 120

The Chinese Mining and Metallurgical Engineering Society is an organization formed by mining and metallurgical engineers, mine owners, and geologists in China. Its main purpose is to study academic knowledge and develop the mining and metallurgical industry. Established for six years, it has published various publications such as the Mining and Metallurgy Magazine, Mining and Metallurgy Special Issue, and the Association Affairs Bi-monthly. All of these publications are written by members of the society and have made significant contributions to mining and metallurgical academic knowledge. The members of the society are scattered throughout the various mining areas of the country. According to the regulations, an annual meeting is held once a year. It is heard that this year's annual meeting has been decided to be held in Hangzhou starting from April 4th. Currently, with the national crisis imminent, discussions will be held on how to organize and collaborate with mining and metallurgical professionals to achieve maximum efficiency during the national mobilization, and how to contribute to the national defense development plan. It is said that the society has over 400 members, and those who have stated their intention to attend the meeting are very enthusiastic. At that time, there will be a grand gathering by the West Lake.

Scheduled Inspection of Salted Pork 121

Starting from April 1st

The issue of inspecting salted pork in the city has recently been approved by the Executive Yuan upon submission by the Municipal Government. Before the Ministry of Industry and Commerce formulates the "Regulations for Domestic Sales Inspection of Goods", the Municipal Health Bureau will temporarily conduct the inspections. The bureau has ordered the Finance, Public Security, and Social Affairs Bureaus to jointly discuss the inspection methods. These bureaus held a joint discussion on March 13th, with representatives from the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau in attendance. It was decided that the inspection will be implemented starting from April 1st. In consideration of the merchants' difficulties, the inspection fee of 50 cents per 100 catties will be reduced to 30 cents. The Municipal Government has approved the proposal for the record, it is said.

Heartless Mother Driven Mad

Actually Planning to Sell Two Daughters into Prostitution 122

Two Daughters File Suit with Uncle and Grandmother

Requesting Approval to Sever Guardianship

Yang Lindi (18 years old) and Yang Jinzhu (16 years old), two sisters residing at No. 11 Xidalu Family House, Yangjing Town, Pudong, together with their uncle Yang Liusheng and grandmother Yang Zhang Shi, have jointly engaged lawyer Qu Yue to file a lawsuit in the civil division of the Second Special District Court against their biological mother Yang Bu Shi (47 years old), who resides at No. 1, Zhicheng Fang, Lan Wei Ai Road, requesting separation and severance of guardianship, etc. The gist of their lawsuit is roughly as follows: "Mediation failed, so we respectfully file a lawsuit, requesting a judgment to prevent degradation and uphold human rights. The First and Second Plaintiffs are the daughters of the Defendant Yang Bu Shi. The bond of kinship will never be forgotten. However, since our late father passed away five years ago and the Defendant has faced difficulties in raising us, the Two Plaintiffs have been working outside to provide some financial support. Recently, the Defendant was misled by others and actually sold the Second Plaintiff to Hailin, a man from Pudong, and a woman named Alin from Ningbo, whose surname is unknown, on the fourth floor of No. 120, Hongyun Fang, Huage Nie Road. It is understood that Alin's mother, a certain old woman, intends to resell the Second Plaintiff into a secret prostitution ring. Once she enters that trap, there is no way to escape. The First Plaintiff overheard the Defendant's plan to take out the Second Plaintiff and then target her as well. She then found out the location of the Second Plaintiff. Initially, she could not find an opportunity, so she returned home. The next day, she went again. Since there were no elders present, they discussed and escaped together, returning to their hometown in Pudong. They tearfully told the Second and Fourth Plaintiffs. They felt that the Defendant's behavior had disgraced the Yang family. Once the First and Second Plaintiffs lost their footing, the regret would last forever. Since we can't avoid things, we requested mediation, hoping for a temporary separation, so that the mother and daughters could return to their original state. The Defendant indicated in court that she would agree. However, after the Defendant agreed, she demanded that a public apology be issued stating that there was no sale. In a family, obedience to elders is paramount. However, in a courtroom, with facts and truth, it is wrong to reverse the situation. Once the report is published, there is a risk of false accusations. The Plaintiffs did not dare to comply, but were willing to publish the mediation record. The Defendant insisted otherwise, resulting in the failure of the mediation, which is a great pity. The court advised us to file another lawsuit to seek legal relief. The Plaintiffs believe that separation and severance of guardianship would not cause any loss to the Defendant. It is better to obey and fall into injustice. Separation is to protect the freedom we were born with. The ancients would accept a small beating, but run away from a big one, so as not to put their parents in an unjust position. The Plaintiffs' humble intentions are also here. Furthermore, on the 9th of this month, the Plaintiffs invited relatives Bu Yunlin, Bu Zhao Gen, Yang Yunbiao, etc., to hold a family meeting. It was resolved to recognize their uncle Yang Liusheng as the guardian of the two of them, in order to take into account both law and emotions, and not to be unfilial. With this unfortunate event, we have found a better way. The Plaintiffs are protected, and the Defendant suffers no loss. Therefore, we request Your Honor to quickly schedule a trial and confirm that the First and Second Plaintiffs are under the guardianship of the Third Plaintiff Yang Liusheng, and to approve the severance of the Defendant's guardianship. The litigation costs should be borne by the Defendant." The Defendant failed to appear at the summons on the afternoon before yesterday. The First, Second, and Third Plaintiffs arrived at court with their lawyer. After Li Liang from the Fourth Division conducted a detailed examination, he scheduled the verdict to be announced on the afternoon of the 31st of this month.

Firing a Gun to Resist Arrest in Pingliang Road

Deputy Detective Shot and Injured 123

One Detective Also Captures Two Robbers Alive

At 9:45 PM last night, the Huishi Police Station on Haining Road suddenly received a secret report stating that several robbers, who had repeatedly committed robbery cases in the police station's jurisdiction and were on the run, were hiding in a shack at the end of Pingliang Road, Yangshupu. After receiving the report, the police station immediately sent Deputy Detective Li Licheng to lead four detectives to secretly arrest them. However, when the detectives arrived at the destination, the robbers had already been alerted and were prepared. When the detectives surrounded the shack from different directions, the robbers opened fire to resist arrest. The detectives also returned fire, and about ten shots were fired in total. Deputy Detective Ji Licheng bravely pursued the robbers amidst the flying bullets and was shot, the bullet entering from below his right neck, causing him to fall to the ground immediately. The remaining detectives continued to press forward. Seeing that the situation was not good, the robbers were about to abandon their guns and flee when two of them were captured alive by the detectives. The rest scattered and fled. The detectives urgently reported to the police station, dispatched a car to take Ji Licheng to the hospital for treatment, and took the two captured robbers back to the police station for detention. They will wait to capture the accomplices before sending them to the court for trial. It is learned that Ji had served as a detective in various police stations. After being promoted to detective captain, he was transferred to the Huishi Police Station. He is a very loyal person and is deeply valued by the authorities. This time, he was injured in the line of duty, and his injuries are quite serious. His life is in danger.

Arrest and Transfer of Liu Yajue in the

Sichuan-Hankou Railway Embezzlement Case 127

Zhang Taijie, the general manager of the Sichuan-Hankou Railway, was sentenced to three years in prison by the Shanghai District Court for embezzling 30,000 yuan of railway funds three years ago. Zhang refused to accept the sentence and appealed to the High Court, which changed the sentence to one year in prison and sent the case back to the Shanghai District Court for execution at the Caohejing Second Prison. He soon died in prison due to illness, and the case was closed. Unexpectedly, there was also a Sichuanese man named Liu Yajue, who was also accused of being an accomplice at the time. The court issued an arrest warrant, but he was not apprehended. Now, Liu, as the plaintiff's agent, was arrested in the Public Concession and handed over to the police station. During the interrogation by the First Special District Court yesterday, the Shanghai District Court sent police to deliver a formal letter and take him back for legal proceedings, it is said.

Letter 134

Dear Sir, Your newspaper's fourteenth page on the twenty-sixth of this month published a news item titled "Bureau of Public Works Approves Price Increase for Chinese Electric Cars," which stated that "the Bureau of Public Works has approved the company to increase the copper round price by two cents uniformly for the first class starting from the next month." After investigation, the Chinese Electric Company has repeatedly submitted applications to increase the price of electric car tickets, all of which have been rejected by this bureau. Recently, the company has requested a reasonable increase in ticket prices on the grounds that the price of copper rounds is depreciating daily and expenses are increasing. The bureau is discussing this matter with the Finance and Public Works Bureau and has not yet approved it. The statement in your newspaper that it has been approved is completely inconsistent with the facts. Please investigate and correct this to avoid confusion. Thank you very much. First Section, Bureau of Public Works, Shanghai Municipality, March 28th, Republic of China, Chen Bao Newspaper Office.

Reader's Consultant 137

Degenerate Family 138

Letter from Qu Zaoqi, Suzhou 丨丨

Editor-in-chief: I am a young man who has just turned twenty. Every time I read your newspaper, I always read the Reader's Consultant first. I am happy to see your insightful opinions and guide young people on the right path. Now I will truthfully tell you about my personal experiences and hope that you can give me a perfect answer. When I was fifteen years old, just after graduating from elementary school, my meddling parents married me to a woman three years older than me who I had never met before. It's a pity that I didn't know what marriage was at that time, which led to today's big mistake! After marriage, because my family situation was still acceptable, I continued my studies. Less than half a year later, my father passed away due to illness. At this time, I was only sixteen years old, and all the family affairs were in my mother's hands. However, my mother was usually idle, and once she took power, she consumed as much as possible. At first, she went in and out of gambling places, then she indulged in opium smoking and spent all day with gentlemen. In addition, after my father passed away, my uncles fought for the property, and lawsuits occurred, so the family fell into bankruptcy. My father's inheritance has almost disappeared so far. Although I struggled to continue my studies, I am now in a provincial vocational school, and there are still more than two years before graduation. During these years, I am preparing to acquire the skills to live independently and get rid of this dark family. Unfortunately, my degenerate mother still feels that her own consumption is not enough. A year ago, she hooked up with a comrade and lived an inhuman life together. Although I have advised her several times, she turned a deaf ear. Knowing that there is no hope, I turned to focus on my wife, hoping to give her all kinds of comfort and encourage each other to strive for the future. However, misfortunes never come singly. My mother has already degenerated, and my wife has followed in her footsteps. This time, when I returned to my hometown during the winter vacation, I contracted gonorrhea, which made my body even weaker. According to medical principles, it is enough to prove that she (referring to my wife) has betrayed me. Although she is an illiterate village girl and the difference in education between us is huge, we have had a history of five or six years together and have a considerable friendship, and she has already given birth to a son and a daughter. I don't have any extravagant expectations, but I really hope that she can be my lifelong companion. Now that she is like this again, what can I do? Because of the mental and physical suffering, my studies and health have been greatly affected. Mr. has seen and heard a lot, is there anyone whose family situation is worse than mine? Now I am determined to study hard so that I can contribute as much as possible to society and ignore everything else. However, can I continue my studies in these few years? Is there a proper way out after graduation? These are important questions. Now I am exposing the dark secrets of my family nakedly, hoping that Mr. has any other good methods and can give me a detailed answer!

Answer: When a family reaches this point, the only thing to do is to sever ties with them decisively. Even if this leads to dropping out of school and becoming a wanderer outside (this is naturally not a good solution, it is best to find a job), it is better than living in that kind of rotten family. As for your wife, if you have a way and are willing to continue your old relationship with her, that would naturally be good, but if this does not happen, you will still not be able to escape the circle of the old family 丨 this would be difficult! Finally, I have one more word of advice for you. Since you have contracted gonorrhea, you should reduce sexual intercourse as much as possible, eat less stimulating foods, and get treatment quickly. It is better to get injections, otherwise, this problem will be more cruel than anything else!

The Jiangsu Education Department Formulated

Standards for Music Teaching Materials 140

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education previously issued a general order to all subordinate departments to submit music teaching materials for review. Recently, at a department affairs meeting, it formulated a standard for music teaching materials, the main purpose of which is to promote nationalistic songs. It ordered all schools to comply with it uniformly. From now on, throughout the north and south of the Yangtze River, only generous and passionate sounds will be heard, and the previously decadent and vulgar songs will be completely eliminated. This is truly a grand event in the education industry. The original standards are recorded as follows:

Standards for Music Teaching Materials for Schools at All Levels in Jiangsu Province 141

A. Music Teaching Materials That Should Be Actively Promoted

(1) Those that promote national spirits such as benevolence, love, peace, bravery, and heroism;

(2) Those that encourage national thoughts such as patriotism, saving the country, and building the country;

(3) Those that cultivate national characteristics such as passion, generosity, endeavor, and progress.

B. Music Teaching Materials That Can Be Selected and Used for Reference

(1) Those that cultivate feelings of harmony, beauty, strength, and composure;

(2) Those that model pure and upright character, noble, independent, and free character;

(3) Pure artistic music with upright style.

C. Music Teaching Materials That Must Be Absolutely Prohibited

(1) Those with romantic, decadent, weak, or vulgar colors;

(2) Those with superstitious, reactionary, or other unreasonable thoughts;

(3) Other music teaching materials that are not suitable for the character and learning ability of young students.

D. Other Points to Note

(1) Chinese songs should be the main focus, and it is not appropriate to sing too many foreign songs, especially foreign songs;

(2) The correct score should be the main focus, Chinese musical instruments should be used as much as possible, and Beijing opera and Kunqu opera should not be used as teaching materials;

(3) Simple classical Chinese or vernacular Chinese should be the main focus, and stiff, archaic, or other difficult words and phrases should be avoided.

Table of Physical Defects in Municipal Schools 155

Should Be Posted in Classrooms of All Levels

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau yesterday issued instructions to the municipal primary and secondary schools in Huhnan, Zhabei, and Pengpu, stating that after the Municipal Health Bureau and the Education Bureau sent personnel to inspect the physical condition of the students in each school, the results are detailed in the health record films. In addition to keeping the record films in the school for future reference, two copies of the student's physical defect and correction record table will be printed and filled out by the school, with one copy submitted to the bureau and the other posted in the classrooms of each level of the school. The purpose is to enable the students themselves and the faculty and staff to pay attention to the correction of students' physical defects and the progress of their health at all times. Schools that have already inspected the physical condition of all students before the New Year can copy the defects of each student into the defect and correction record table according to the existing records and post them in the classrooms separately. As for the re-examination of the physical condition of old students, it will be implemented after the number of school health workers is slightly increased. These instructions are hereby issued for your information.
