China-Portugal Football Match Scheduled 161

April 9th and 15th

The rumor of the resumption of the China-Portugal Cup football match has been reported in the previous newspapers. Now, the sports authorities of China and Portugal are making every effort to promote this matter. It was originally planned to be held at present, but the continuous spring rain has prevented the Western League and the Chinese Football Association from finishing on schedule. Therefore, the competition has to be postponed slightly. According to the notification from the Chinese Sports Association yesterday, it has been decided to hold it on April 9th (Sunday) and April 15th (Saturday) at the China National Amateur Athletic Federation's athletic field on Route Pere Robert. During this bright spring season for sports, the focus will shift accordingly. The football season is coming to an end, but unexpectedly there will be a grand football match to reward the fans, which is a feast for the eyes.

A Brief History of the China-Portugal Cup: As for the history of the China-Portugal Cup, it has been reported in this newspaper. The cup was donated by the Portuguese Sports Association of Shanghai, worth more than 300 gold pieces, for three matches and two wins, in order to promote the friendship between the two countries in sports and to learn from each other. Each year, a three-match, two-win system is adopted to determine the annual winner. If a team wins consecutively for three years, it will be honored to permanently preserve the cup. In the past, the two countries have each won one year. This year is the final key to the cup's gain or loss, and both sides will compete with all their strength.

Comparison of the Strengths of China and Portugal: The strength between the two countries is very strong. The Chinese team has the Donghua and Youyou Jinan teams, which won the Western League Group A championship, with many good generals and talents. Portugal won the Shanghai International Football Championship in 1929, and its reputation has long been established. Almost everyone who knows the history of football in Shanghai knows this. In recent years, it seems to have faded and declined, but the veterans are still scattered among the strong teams of the Western League, such as the French Business Association, which has strong combat effectiveness and outstanding results. Most of its players are Portuguese, such as Marcel, Remydi, and Favanque, all of whom are famous generals. Once China and Portugal go to war, the outcome is unpredictable, and the grand occasion can be expected.

Announced by the Municipal Education Bureau

Regulations for the 2nd Joint Middle School Games 162

To be Held for Three Days from April 27th to 29th

The Sports Games are Divided into Two Parts: Group Exercises and Track and Field Events

Separate Awards will be Given for Men's and Women's Eight Championships and Group Exercises

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, in order to hold the city's second joint middle school games, issued a notice yesterday, stating that the bureau will hold the city's second joint middle school games from April 27th to 29th to promote sports in middle schools citywide. The regulations have been drafted, submitted to the municipal government for approval and announced under Order No. 5359. This notice is issued to announce the regulations to all schools. Included are copies of the regulations.

Regulations for the 2nd Joint Middle School Games of Shanghai

Article 1: This event is sponsored by the Municipal Education Bureau and aims to promote sports in middle schools citywide. Article 2: All municipal and private middle schools in the city that have been approved for establishment must have students participate as athletes in this event. However, other public middle schools in the city may also select students to apply to participate as athletes in this event. Article 3: The venue for this event will be the athletic field of the China National Amateur Athletic Federation on Route Pere Robert. Article 4: The opening date of this event is from April 27th to April 29th, 1933. If necessary, the president of this event may decide to change it. Article 5: The mayor will serve as the president of this event, and the director of the Education Bureau will serve as the vice president. Article 6: This event will have a director in charge of all event affairs, and will be divided into two departments: administrative and athletic. Each department will have a secretary-general. The administrative department will have six sections: general affairs, accounting, documentation, editing, reception, and discipline. The athletic department will have two sections: competition and venue. All staff will be appointed by the director of the Education Bureau. Article 7: The sports games are divided into two parts: group exercises and track and field events. The items are as follows: A. Group Exercises Department: (1) Grand Assembly Exercise: Each school should participate with one-tenth of its total student population as representatives. (2) Group Exercises: such as Chinese martial arts, walking, calisthenics, games, apparatus exercises, fitness dances, etc. B. Track and Field Department: (1) Men's: Field events: high jump, long jump, pole vault, discus throw, javelin throw, shot put. Track events: 100 meters, 200 meters, 400 meters, 800 meters, 1500 meters, 110-meter hurdles, 800-meter relay race, 1600-meter relay race. (2) Women's: Field events: high jump, long jump, javelin throw, shot put. Track events: 50 meters, 100 meters, 200 meters, 400-meter relay race. (3) The above men's and women's track and field events will be held in two groups, A and B. The grouping criteria will be determined separately. Article 8: Each track and field athlete may register for no more than three events, except for relay races. Each school may have no more than three participants per event in each department. Article 9: The competition rules shall be in accordance with the competition rules of the China National Amateur Athletic Federation. All athletes should strictly abide by and unconditionally accept the results of the referees. Article 10: There are eight types of track and field championships in this event, including four types each for men's and women's A and B group team and individual. 1. The team championship will be awarded to the school with the most points. If two or more schools have the same number of points, the school with the most first-place finishes will be the winner. 2. The individual championship will be awarded to the athlete with the most points. If two or more athletes have the same number of points, the athlete with the most first-place finishes will be the winner, and so on. Article 11: Awards will be given to those with excellent performances in group exercises. Article 12: The competition methods for middle school sports schools in this city participating in various track and field events will be determined separately. Article 13: These regulations will be implemented after approval and promulgation by the Municipal Education Bureau and the Municipal Government.

China-England International Shooting Competition

The Situation Between the Two Sides is Gradually Tense

Today, Zhang Yingda Faces Niemann

A Pair of Veteran Soldiers on the Battlefield... Striving for Victory

Yesterday's Results: Chinese Liu Zongfu Disappointed, British Packer Particularly Good

1000 Points to 711 Points, a Defeat of 289 Points

The Total Number of Points for the Two Days Shows That China Still Leads by 104 Points

In the China-England International Shooting Competition, today is the third day, and the situation between the two sides is gradually tense. Today, the Chinese and English representatives Zhang Yingda and Niemann are both veterans of the battlefield, and each will strive for victory for their country. On the first day, Xu Shizhang won 393 points for China. Yesterday, Liu changed his usual state and suffered at the hands of the enemy, losing 289 points. The total number of points for the two days shows that China still leads by 104 points.

Packer's Performance Was Particularly Good 163

All those watching from the sidelines unanimously praised the performance of British Packer. The second half was particularly good. Before the last shot to reach the goal was finished, there were already as many as 95 points. Therefore, Liu Zongfu's failure was not simply due to bad luck. Packer's huge scores that day, such as 32, 61, 32, 81, 77, and 95, were on average more impressive than in the past. His maturity and steadiness were well-deserved. Within the first ten shots of the first half, he had not yet gained momentum. Around twenty shots, he began to advance fiercely and took the lead with 293 to 144. He suddenly suffered a blow and fell behind again. Near the end, he won another 23 points (500 to 477), and in the second half he continued to add points, gaining 81 points and seizing the superior position. From then on, he had smooth sailing, and by the end, before the last shot was finished, he had already won by 289 points.

Liu Zongfu Changed His Usual State 164

Liu Zongfu's usual performance is superior to that of his opponent. Generally, people thought that Liu's chances of victory were greater. Even Packer regarded him as a strong opponent and was unwilling to let him go easily. However, Liu suddenly changed his usual state and suffered setbacks one after another. The reason was also that he was competing for the first time in a formal competition, and he was inevitably flustered in the face of the battle. Observing him not long after the start of the match, the gun and bullets failed to cooperate, and he wandered on a divergent path, not knowing where to go. He continued to lose as much as 150 points. Fortunately, he turned back in time, calmed his will, first firmly defended, repelling the enemy from thousands of miles away, and then, when there was an opportunity, he attacked, increasing his score. In the third set of three-five, two-three, and four-six, he suddenly took the lead, gaining fifty points. The good times did not last, and Liu fell into a state of confusion again, leading to a complete downfall. In the second half, Liu tried to remain calm, but it was difficult to do as he wished. He sighed and returned in disappointment. There are many days to come, and Liu should make redoubled efforts to avenge his previous shame.

Municipal Education Bureau Yesterday

Held a Sports Lecture 165

Invited Mr. Shen Siliang to Speak

And Held a Certificate and Award Ceremony

The Municipal Education Bureau held a sports lecture and awarded certificates of qualification to the health personnel training class and prizes to the winners of the health speech contest yesterday afternoon from 2:30 PM in the auditorium of Wuben Girls' Middle School. Li Ting'an, director of the Municipal Health Bureau, Zhou Feicheng, section chief of the Municipal Education Bureau, Ma Chonggan, Zhou Shang, Lu Bingyun, Li Wanyu, Wang Keyong, and other standing committee members of the health education committee sports group, as well as principals and physical education teachers of public and private primary and secondary schools in the city, graduates of the health personnel training class, and winners of the health speech contest, totaling more than 500 people, attended. The details are divided and recorded as follows:

The Situation of Awarding Prizes: After Chairman Zhou Feicheng performed the ceremony, the chairman first reported on the process of running the health training class and the health speech contest. Then, Director Li Ting'an of the Health Bureau delivered a training speech, roughly stating that health is closely related to the survival of individuals, society, and the nation. There are many reasons for China's current national crisis, but the unhealthy psychology and unhealthy bodies of the Chinese people are a major reason. Because of unhealthy psychology, phenomena such as irresponsibility and selfishness occur. Because of unhealthy bodies, there is a lack of vigor and spirit in doing things, and phenomena such as fear and contentment in the face of things occur. The health training class and speech contest held by the Education and Health Bureaus are not effective enough to be universal, so I hope that everyone will study without being confined to their location and spread and develop it from the sea to the whole country in order to achieve great results. Finally, Chairman Zhou Feicheng issued certificates of qualification for the health class, certificates of merit for the first place in the examination of the health class in each district, and certificates of merit and medals for the winners of the speech contest. Then, the meeting was photographed and dismissed.

Shen Siliang's Lecture: After the awarding of prizes, Dr. Shen Siliang spoke on the theory and practice of physical education for young people and children, roughly stating that life is divided into four major periods: infancy, childhood, adulthood, and old age. The so-called young people and children are between the ages of one and twenty, accounting for one-third of their lives. If young people cannot be properly educated, it will be enough to affect their whole lives, and physical education is the movement of life, which is related whether in the reading era or the old age. Our daily movements and habits are customary and unconscious, which are habits formed from childhood. If good habits are not formed in childhood, they will not be easily changed in the future, so everyone should first pay attention to cultivating good habits in children. Chinese physical education has always paid attention to the abnormal development of championship teams, etc., which is especially inappropriate for children. Therefore, primary school teachers must provide comprehensive training for children's physical education, using their playful nature to guide them, and should have a good sports environment, comparison of group sports, encouragement of prizes, etc., in order to arouse children's interest in physical education.

Questions for Discussion: For example, primary schools suggest: (1) What are the minimum number of sports equipment that should be used in primary schools? (2) What is appropriate for boarding students in rural schools to do morning exercises and interval exercises? (3) What kind of games are appropriate for boys and girls to exercise together? Mr. Shen answered: (1) It should be based on the amount of school funding and the number of students. It is best to use 10% to 15% of the school's funding for sports equipment. (2) If there are no morning exercises or interval exercises, it is also appropriate. (3) Students over the age of ten should exercise separately because of the different natures of boys and girls. Finally, Shao Rugan of the Education Bureau explained the teaching materials for the assembly exercise and discussed various issues of the second sports games, and then dismissed the meeting.

Free Talk

On Achieving Resistance Capability 174

Speaking of resisting Japan and saving the nation, the best method is naturally "long-term resistance." However, long-term resistance is not easy. It requires not only the determination to resist, but also the "capability to resist." We have certainly had the "determination" for a long time. The central government has repeatedly stated that it "already has the determination," and in the letters and telegrams of the generals, all righteously and indignantly stated, "To die for the country is to live forever, even in death," showing that we have long possessed "determination." What we lack now is only the "capability to resist."

"Saving the nation without following the right path, struggling without proper methods," everyone only knows to blindly save the nation, and engage in clamorous struggles. The "result of resistance" is that it "does not harm the enemy's slightest hair." Therefore, resistance must first have the capability to resist; otherwise, "the country will still be destroyed." It would be better to adopt non-resistance.

What is "resistance capability"? It is:

First, it is "having received national education and possessing the spirit of the National Revolutionary Army." "We often see those whose material resources are inferior to others but whose spirit surpasses them achieving victory." (Note by Da: like the A-Q type).

Second, it is "enriching the nation's production capacity (Note by Da: such as planting ××, etc.), and then thinking of various methods (methods detailed later) to make the nation's production capacity applicable as military force." (Note by Da: such as ×× public sales, etc.).

The first item is "spiritual education," which is most beneficial for long-term resistance. "Ten years of training," that's what it means. Anyone can understand it at a glance. The second item is not only a military issue, but also involves political, social, and other issues, which seems more difficult to understand. Since it has already been clearly stated to enrich the nation's production capacity, and that material is inferior to spirit has also been established as a law, then what is to be produced here is probably and certainly "spiritual production." What is spiritual production? It is still nothing more than the "determination" for long-term resistance and the "confidence" of ascending to heaven after death. As for the so-called various methods, they are nothing more than issuing national salvation bonds, collecting national salvation donations, and launching the aviation national salvation movement initiated by the people, etc., etc.

National salvation bonds are issued by the government, and national salvation donations can be advanced by each province in different ways. As for aviation national salvation, it is an extra contribution, and regardless of wealth or poverty, everyone naturally has the obligation to "contribute money." In this way, the determination to resist exists, and the capability to resist also exists. From now on, we should have no worries about the country's destruction. As for "weak physical strength and high blood pressure," that doesn't matter, because spirit ultimately prevails over matter.

Li Huiying on the Riverbank 175

A person quietly walked to the riverbank and stood there blankly.

Let me count it. Ah, it's been more than thirteen months since I left this place. After a long absence, I really don't know how happy I am! Especially the warm spring sun, which makes people feel lazy, and from time to time there is a breeze blowing from the sea and from the fields, which simply intoxicates people.

I opened my eyes, which had been restricted by the city for thirteen months, and looked at the opposite riverbank as I had done thirteen months ago. Nothing has changed, the opposite riverbank! There are still green trees, still green fields, still a patch of beach emerging on the riverbank, and there are still the thatched sheds that some people consider unsightly and the smoke constantly rising from the thatched sheds, with a blue sky setting off the distant places behind.

Looking out at the sea, it is just as it used to be, a large expanse of bright white and dark water, with the sky and water tightly connected, sailboats, steamers, and the Empress constantly coming and going, and even the seabirds skimming the water still show their sweet smiles of the past.

After thirteen months of separation, my riverbank, where I used to swim for four years, has not changed much.

Really, nothing has changed? No, there are some differences after all. As soon as I saw the large gap in the riverbank at my feet, I remembered that it was indeed different. There is no doubt that it was bombarded by the artillery fire of Japanese imperialism. This huge scar, however, has grown green grass after thirteen months. Perhaps, after some time, the scar will completely change and not attract anyone's attention. However, I can never forget it!

Turning around to look at the area behind me, there are many more different places: in the distance, Wusong Town presents a scene of rubble, the red brick buildings of the university hall still have the walls after the bombing, and the radio station has only one iron pole left; nearby, the dilapidated station and the completely burned thatched houses! Now only a flat ground remains, the missing seaside hotel and exquisite bungalows, and the many familiar faces of the past, students, villagers, playful children, station staff, policemen, and even a few familiar village dogs are gone, not to be seen. How can it be said that it is the same as before?

Isn't all of this a gift from the "January 28th Incident"? Thirteen months ago, wasn't this place the scene of the Japanese imperialist war of aggression every day? Airplanes, bombs, artillery, and machine guns flew, roared, and bombed, turning the area along the riverbank, houses, livestock, and people into ruins.

But these are still visible traces. As for those anti-imperialist warriors who fought for national survival, their sacrificed lives and their shed red blood, are there no traces of them now? And who would think of these things? Hasn't even a painting of broken walls and ruins been left behind?

"It doesn't matter," I thought. "Soldiers are bound to die sooner or later, and they died in the anti-imperialist war, which is very glorious, isn't it? And," I changed my mind again, "isn't it because they were not afraid of death that they created a few national heroes for our Republic of China? That China, a colonized country, would produce a few national heroes. Wouldn't that make everything easier? Wouldn't that bring glory to the international community as well!"

Alas, I really don't know where the souls of these dead warriors (if they really have souls) have gone. Perhaps they are complaining and regretting their deaths...

Forget it, don't look anymore, don't think anymore. A person quietly walked down the riverbank and headed home. At this moment, in my heart, there was a kind of indescribable pain.

Wang Wanrong, the Nun Daosu 176

Daosu is dead. From now on, the nightingale's singing will no longer be heard in the Nunnery of Chastity, and the fragrance of white lotuses will no longer be smelled!

I met Daosu in the late spring four years ago.

The Nunnery of Chastity is at the foot of Qin Mountain. Although it was late spring, there was still no murmur of birds or fragrant flowers. Only a bright, beaded waterfall flowed straight down from Qin Mountain like falling clouds and scattered cotton. After falling to the ground, it flowed right in front of the nunnery. On both sides of the nunnery, there were towering ancient trees, and in a tomb among the ancient trees lay a deceased old nun. Standing in the main hall of the Nunnery of Chastity, we could hear the gurgling of the spring and the surging of the pine waves. Therefore, the nuns in the nunnery were not very lonely. This place was not as gloomy as other nunneries, like an ancient tomb.

Daosu was a thin little nun. No one knew her background, and no one knew when she became a nun. She was good at closing her eyes and sighing with her eyebrows raised. Her pure white face and delicate body made one think of a white lotus in clear water at first sight. And when she sat cross-legged in front of the idol, reaching out from the black, wide cassock and gently tapping the wooden fish, chanting scriptures in a melodious voice, her leisurely demeanor and clear voice made one think of the low singing of a nightingale under the moon. Who says the Nunnery of Chastity is lonely? There is the gurgling of the spring and the surging of the pine waves. Who says it is always winter in the Nunnery of Chastity? Where does the low singing of the nightingale and the faint fragrance of the white lotus come from in winter?

Now, two years have passed. The gurgling of the spring is still there, and the surging of the pine waves remains. But the singing of the nightingale can no longer be heard, and the fragrance of the white lotus can no longer be smelled!

Daosu! If you also have a soul that exists in another world, I hope there are also pine waves, streams, clear breezes, and bright moons there, and you can still sing like a nightingale and sway like a white lotus!

The Philosophy of Life by Yang Liuan 177

Those who study philosophy are almost always said to be crazy because these things have nothing to do with firewood, rice, oil, and salt. However, the "philosophy of life" is indispensable!

Some doctors and scholars initially really went to study some "outlines" and some "histories" in a dull-headed way, but after understanding the "philosophy of life," they immediately threw these things aside. This is because these things are only good for people to use as toilet paper and do not quite coincide with the first chapter of "The ABCs of Getting Promoted and Making a Fortune" in the "philosophy of life." Getting promoted and making a fortune, the shortcut lies in Zhongnan Mountain.

What is the shortcut? Nothing else, "flattery" and "bragging." Everyone can do "flattery" and "bragging," but the skills are different. For example, the League of Nations investigation report, written for foreign dignitaries and pleasing to the local government, must show the spirit of "independence" and say repeatedly, "Excellent, excellent! Justice prevails, and reason is upheld!" This is the positive way of flattering. (Choosing foreign horses to flatter is an even more powerful method.) For example, some people want to fight for the protection of civil rights, and you want to please the government, so you say, "Civil rights are tied to the law. Once the constitution is successful, civil rights will naturally be protected. You cannot think from a political standpoint, but must demand from a legal standpoint. (Isn't the government clearly drafting a constitution?! But this sentence cannot be explicitly stated.)" This is the way of implying flattery.

As for "bragging," for example, you can say that any old novel is good. Write a preface to that novel, describing it in a dazzling way, and then "curious" people will fall into your trap, and then you can get a sum of writing fees from the cracks in the book buying. For example, if you "brag" yourself into a world scholar, a first-class celebrity, someone will invite you to give a lecture, and then you can brag again, and each time you can get a "travel expense" of 5,000 silver dollars.

These are just two examples. In fact, there are many other methods. But in short, both "flattery" and "bragging" must have one condition: a thick face. And you also have to be able to "endure." For example, if you are given a position like Minister of Education, it is best not to do it, because there are better things than that. You might as well wait.

With all these methods, the "philosophy of life" is accomplished. A "verse" is composed:

The philosophy of life is to seek fame and profit. To seek fame and profit, flatter and brag. Your face must be thick, and your heart must be soft. "Independent," "bragging," and "flattering" are different from ordinary people. This is how I see it: How fitting, how fitting! Why is it not fitting?

The Age of Long Creative Works and the Crossroads of Love by Zhang Ping 178

"Where did you go in China? Why don't you keep to the time?"

As soon as Tang Yaoxing picked him up, he asked him with a half-smiling, half-annoyed pinching of his lips.

"I went to see a movie."

Haiquan replied with a smile, and saw that there were two young men he did not know sitting in Tang Yaoxing's room.

"You are really a little bourgeois, a leisure class!"

Yaoxing scolded him with a smile. But Haiquan just smiled. Stepping into the room, he asked the two young men sitting there for their names.

"Let me introduce you..."

Tang Yaoxing laughed before he spoke.

"...This Mr. Zheng Jiaqi is a feudal remnant from Zhejiang. This Mr. Liu Songxin is a local tyrant from Shanxi... This is... is a compradore class, a pretty boy from Guangdong, Mr. Lin Haiquan..."

"Nonsense! How am I a compradore class?"

So the four of them burst into laughter.

"There's good news tonight... Let's go quickly, let's call a car to go faster."

"What's the good news?"

"Mr. Chen will report to us after we get there."

They all fell silent and walked out together. Tang Yaoxing went to a car dealership to call a car. The three of them just stood at the entrance of the alley and waited for him.

"Where are we going?"

Haiquan asked them.

"I don't know either."

Zheng Jiaqi replied with a smile.

"I heard we're going to a foreign hotel."

After that, there was silence. In a moment, the car that Tang Yaoxing was sitting in drove up. The three of them got into the car.

"Where to?"

Haiquan heard the driver asking Yaoxing. Yaoxing answered the driver in a very low voice. Haiquan couldn't hear clearly where he said to go.

Random Notes

Mussolini Apologizes to a Young Friend 204

— Zhan Lu

The world-renowned Italian Premier Mussolini, wrote a letter to a Swiss child scolding him: Why has there been no news to this day about the hand organ purchased from a certain Italian factory? Mr. Mussolini did not hesitate to humble himself and write a personal letter of apology, stating that the factory had gone bankrupt, causing the young friend to hope; he specially sent a hand organ as a token of apology and asked the young friend to forgive the delay, and so on. The Swiss child would be mischievous and did not complain to the factory owner for failing to buy the hand organ, but asked the prime minister about it. If according to the officialdom customs of the East, it would have been ignored long ago; or, write a sentence: No need to bother. Or, write a sentence: Let the children negotiate with the factory themselves. Below this is not this comment, it must be this decree, if it is not written on a pink card, it must be pasted on the front wall. If you want to teach him to apologize to the children in writing, it is like hanging a fish on his nose, forget about it.

Mr. [Mussolini] is willing to apologize to a young friend, after all, he is a premier with "tolerance." But, when Mr. Mussolini was a child himself, he was also a mischievous child. He was short in stature as a child, and his eyes were full of sharp energy. When he was twelve or thirteen years old and was ordered by his father to go to the provincial capital, a classmate insulted him, and he pulled out his small pocket knife to stab his first enemy. Mr. Mussolini was so strict with children in his childhood, but so humble with children as premier. This is a question worth discussing.

In the 1919 Italian election, the Socialist Party rose to prominence, and Mussolini's Fascists were defeated. The Socialist Party triumphantly paraded through the city, shouting "Death to Mussolini" under the banners flying. Mussolini, sitting in the offices of the People's Daily, pointed to the pistol on the desk and said to the editor, "Aren't they just a bunch of blind thugs under their banners? If they come here, I will kill them, I'm just afraid they don't have the courage." Mussolini refused to show weakness to the shouts of the Socialist Party in his disappointment, but Mussolini was willing to plead guilty to the accusations of children in his success. This is another question worth discussing.

The Essence of General Qi's Courage Training 205

— Qing Qu

The other day, I happened to flip through Qi Jiguang's book "Record of Practical Training of Soldiers", which contained "First, train soldiers; second, train courage; third, train ears and eyes; fourth, train hands and feet; fifth, train camps and formations; sixth, train generals." These six training methods are certainly not suitable for the current enemy's strong army and sophisticated equipment. But speaking of "training courage", I think it is the same from ancient times to the present, and it is worth putting forward for the main leaders who hold military power and lead the war of resistance against Japan to choose from. It is also a very good commentary.

What is "training courage" for? In the past, military equipment only included bows, arrows, shields, spears, halberds, axes, and huge swords. Now, in addition to guns and cannons, airplanes are used for bombing. When the rumbling sound is overhead and the soldiers standing on the front line encounter missiles raining down and flames clouding over, they will instantly become a pile of ruins, even if they are hiding in deep trenches and high fortresses. May I ask if the life and death of the front-line troops can be determined in an instant? Therefore, at this time, they must still be ordered to charge desperately, like an "resolutely fearless, as safe as walking on flat ground", so that they will not "shudder without being cold and collapse without fighting". How can they do it? Tang Yulin's abandonment of the city and escape is the most recent example. Others say that he sold out the country after receiving bribes, resulting in the loss of the army and the loss of territory. In fact, relying on an isolated city, even with natural dangers, he did not have the "courage" to defend it. It is heard that his troops, who were the last to escape, were also killed by enemy soldiers, and the bullets entered from behind. Isn't this evidence of cowardice and retreat?

Therefore, I say that Qi Jiguang's "Record of Practical Training of Soldiers" is indeed a valuable military book, but training soldiers, of course, should take "training courage" as the first priority. Furthermore, if the soldiers' courage has been strengthened, but the generals' courage has not been trained, it is still useless. Why? The general in command of the army must go to the front line to command. If, when fighting with the enemy, he hears the sound of guns and cannons, which is louder than thunder, he will cover his ears and flee. Even if he advances, he will turn around and avoid it when he sees that the place reached by the artillery fire has become a bloody road. I am afraid that his expression will change and his behavior will inevitably be in a panic. At this point, the generals are like this, can the soldiers still fight to the death and fight the enemy to the death? Training soldiers requires "training courage", and training generals also requires "training courage". When Qi Jiguang of the Ming Dynasty was able to resist Japan and dare not invade our Central Plains, and the Qi family army and the Yue family army shone in succession, it was precisely because of this. I hope that those in charge of military administration now also adopt this essence to revitalize the declining morale.

When the Swallows Fly to Jiangnan 206

— Huo Ming

Ou Yangxieu's swallow poem has two lines: "Always towards spring and autumn club before and after, for whom to return and for whom to come." Now that the spring breeze is clear and warm, and the countryside is full of flowers, it is already the Cold Food Festival, when the swallows start from the warm land and fly to Jiangnan.

We see each other only once a year. Although we don't understand what they are murmuring, we always feel that this sound is very familiar and very beautiful. When I was a child, I lived in a small village on the coast of the East China Sea. Three or five swallow nests were arranged on the beams of a tile house. From the time the autumn wind rises and the swallows return to the south, I feel lonely, until in mid-spring, when the peach blossoms in Jiangnan are about to bloom and the rape flowers are in full bloom, they will fly in groups as usual and live with us. Every morning, they chirp happily, waking me up from my dream, and I immediately get up, stand in the sunlight to watch them fly, and listen to their whispers. At noon, facing the river, I also appreciate them busily weaving in the blue water shadow like shuttles. Two spring petals fall on their black scissor wings. As long as they turn over their snow-egg-like belly, like magic, the fallen flowers fly open, and they slip across the water and disappear into the willows. In the evening, watching the old swallows bring things back, I once wrote a short poem:

"Eaves hovering, flying near the nest then turning back. Inducing all the chicks to stick out their heads, remotely gazing at their foraging mother returning." This mood of village life cannot be recovered now. I seem to be sitting in this ruined city of Shanghai, without seeing peach blossoms or swallows.

However, the swallow nests in the market have been trafficked from the villages of my hometown to Shanghai [?] I am stirring up my homesickness with a pale heart, and I cherish the death of my youth even more. Ah, swallow! Just like you, I am flying back and forth in the whirlpool of life in a hurry, and I am also wasting my dreamlike hopes. But what is the point? Like you, I no longer have a home!

The Elite of the Crash Course 208

— Zhou Jingzhi

This is how Bai Wei and Ms. Qin Xiang started their acquaintance: One morning, bathed in the allure of spring, Bai Wei, having no classes at school, planned to visit his close friend, Lao Chen, at Xiushan Park. When he stepped into Lao Chen's room, he found two young and beautiful ladies. One was Lao Chen's wife, Ms. C, whom he had known for a long time. The other, however, was someone he had never met. "Is Lao Chen not at home?"

"He hasn't returned since last night. Ah, let me introduce you. This is Comrade Bai Wei, a person of great renown in literary circles. This is Ms. Qin Xiang, a highly celebrated socialite, the 'Empress of Shanghai.'"

"I have long admired you, your name precedes you like thunder." And with that, they understood each other tacitly.

××××××

A week later, their footprints were already on the dance floor, they were seen wandering in the park day and night, their emotions were blazing, and they were busy renting a house and buying furniture, hastily building a small family to live out their monotonous lives.

××××××

Another week later, their emotions cooled, because their personalities clashed, leading to frequent disagreements, making it difficult to continue living together. Eventually, they hired a lawyer and declared bankruptcy and divorce. This young couple, from meeting to divorce, took only a month. In this great China, where everyone is chanting "Crash Course ××" and "Crash Course ××," they can be considered to have deeply understood the essence of it all, the elite of the crash course.

A Long Novel

The Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 209

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 3: Finally Bearing the Heart to Untie the Bell, He Enters the Door; Mistakenly Pities the Maiden and Wishes to Share Her Food

Therefore, without hesitation, he went straight to the Yang family. Reaching the outer room, he first called out with a smile, "Old Madame!" He always greeted her this way. This call of "Old Madame" was not a respectful address, but merely a telegram from an old maid, telling her, "I have arrived." After each such greeting, Gui Zhi would invariably come out silently, nodding and smiling. Without saying "Welcome," the full extent of her warm welcome was naturally expressed without any reservation. But today, after this call of "Old Madame," the situation changed drastically. From inside the room, someone asked sternly, "Who is it?" This "Who?" was called out by Gui Zhi. Given how well he and Gui Zhi knew each other, would Gui Zhi not recognize his voice? Moreover, this "Who?" was asked with great emphasis, not at all like a casual inquiry. This was quite strange, why was it so? This was a representation never before seen since they knew each other! Just as he was puzzling over this, Jiang said from inside, "Is it Second Master Gan? Please come in." Ji Zhi responded and walked in, only to see the old maid sitting on the kang with her head lowered, her eyes red. Jiang stood up to greet him, smiling, "Second Master, did our girl offend someone in your household?" Upon hearing this, Ji Zhi knew that something had happened, and his face reddened as well, but he deliberately calmed himself and feigned ignorance, asking, "What makes you say that?" Jiang said, "Today…" Gui Zhi, looking upset, repeatedly tugged at her mother's clothes, pouting, "Why are you saying so much? Don't say it, don't say it!" Jiang said, "Second Master hasn't offended you, why can't we say it? Even if Second Master has offended you, we still have to ask for a clear explanation." Hearing her mother explain it this way, Gui Zhi lowered her head and remained silent. Jiang smiled, "Second Master, don't take it to heart. We are poor people, and orphans and widows at that, how dare we argue with anyone? But we have to make things clear. We may be poor, but we are an honest family. Although we make some clothes for your household to make a living, that is our duty. If your household says that my daughter and I don't do a good job, then you can just stop having us make clothes. But we haven't done anything wrong. Today, my girl went to your household, intending to ask the Madam if the clothes made by Second Master fit well or not. This is just her being overly attentive." (26)

Whereabouts

A Small Record of Travels To and From Xinshu 210

— Ke Ding

(Part 1)

Xinshu is another name for Xinshi, and it also has a name called "Xiantan" (Fairy Pool). In the Xinshi Town Gazetteer, there are many records of mythological legends. I will not mention it now and leave it for another time. Xinshi is the largest town under the jurisdiction of Deqing County in Zhejiang Province, and its customs and people are excellent models. The famous painter Shen Quan, also known as Nanping, of the Qing Dynasty, was also from Xinshi!

I went to Xinshi when I was three years old, so Xinshi is also my second hometown, and my relationship with it is very close. What I can't forget about Xinshi is the Lion Peak on Guoshan outside Nan Zha, also known as Jiashan (Fake Mountain), the Beauty Stone, and Taoyuan (Peach Blossom Spring). And the two Great Vajras of Juehai Temple in the center of the town. (See details below.)

The Lion Peak of Guoshan is a lion-shaped rock, with its head raised towards the east, mouth open and eyes glaring. When you look at it in the morning, it seems as if it wants to swallow the bright red sun in one gulp. Its posture is majestic and its spirit is uplifting, but the idle class who are generally indifferent will certainly not think of these things. The Beauty Stone is also almost there, with a graceful demeanor, as if Xishi (a famous beauty in ancient China) is slowly coming. Taoyuan Cave is a few steps further, and it is a stone cave about eight feet wide, with a flat stone slab on top and soft green grass around it. However, it is said that there are ghosts below, so no one has ever ventured down to this day. The two Great Vajras of Juehai Temple were made by a certain doctor Li near Xinshi. He was also in high spirits and joked with the famous craftsmen from Jiangxi (Jiangxi has famous sculptors. When Xinshi was building Juehai Temple, they went to invite several to sculpt the Four Great Vajras). During the sculpting process, both sides kept secrets, surrounding the area with dense bamboo fences to prevent anyone from seeing it. On the day the great work was completed, the bamboo fences were removed, and everyone admired it. Who knew that the Jiangxi masters, whom the people of Xinshi usually worshiped, had completely collapsed, while the unknown Li was praised by the public. It turned out that what he sculpted was full of spirit and lifelike, while what the Jiangxi people sculpted was ordinary and sleepy. So these few things can occupy my mind.

(Part 2)

My second hometown, for a cost of less than three yuan, is now before my eyes, and the tall Buyun Bridge is still intact. But everything else shows a very sad image. Last year, the farmers had a bumper harvest of all grains, and their hearts were so open and their families were so happy. Who knew that all places had bumper harvests, and everyone couldn't sell their crops for a good price. So a new term was created: "Cheap grain hurts farmers." Xinshi also felt the economic downturn due to "cheap grain hurting farmers." Usually, the people in the town cursed the people in the countryside, but now they have no reason to curse. It is said that:

"Two South Goods stores, two silk stores, one dim sum shop, and one teahouse... have all announced the cessation of business!"

If you walk on the street, you will feel like you are in a "dead city," but I know deeply that this is a universal phenomenon, not just Xinshi.

The Lion Peak in front of Guoshan is still raising its head to swallow the sun, the Beauty Stone is still slender in attitude, and Taoyuan Cave is still the same; but the two Great Vajras of Juehai Temple have more traces of peeling, like the scars of our Northeast.

The people of Xinshi are patriotic and do not want to lag behind. In a few days, there will be a drama to raise funds for "National Salvation Through Aviation." It is said that it will not be officially implemented until after the traditional opera performance at the beginning of the third lunar month. "National Salvation Through Aviation" is the highest method of saving the country. It is expected that many people in Xinshi will open their wallets to go there!

On the evening of the 22nd, it was said that the small steamer from Hangzhou to Xin was robbed, and one passenger was injured. This is also an important issue that researchers of social problems need to study urgently.

The injury on my right hand, , hurts, cannot move, and is ice-cold. Thanks to my friend Mr. Gu's one or two injections, it gradually loosened. It was really only three days! I was able to hold a pen a little. So I hurried to Shanghai.

Military Operations in Eastern Rehe Have Been Launched 211

The Enemy Attacks Our Positions on the East Bank of the Shi River

Fierce Fighting Near Jiǔménkǒu

The Japanese Side Plans to Actively Expand the Scope of the War

Large Numbers of Enemy Aircraft Bombard Near Jianchangying and Fly South of Qian'an for Reconnaissance

(Beiping) Last night, more than 100 enemies from Huimazhai on the east bank of the Shi River attacked our Dingshan position on the east bank. Our troops fought back bravely and repelled the enemy after a fierce battle. On the left flank of Shimenzhai, one of our battalions made contact with the enemy's forward units. The fighting was extremely fierce, and they are still in a stalemate this morning. (29th Dispatch)

(Linyu) At about 5:00 AM on the 28th, more than 100 enemy infantrymen were spotted advancing towards our position in front of Huimazhai on the east bank of the Shi River. They immediately clashed with our sentries, killing four or five enemies. They are currently facing each other across the Shi River. At the same time, a train of enemy armored vehicles was active back and forth east of the Shi River railway bridge. At about 11:00 AM, more than 20 more enemies searched and advanced towards our Shi River position and were also calmly repelled by our guards. At noon, an enemy plane came to Haiyang, Qinhuangdao, and the Shi River area for reconnaissance for a long time and did not drop bombs before flying east. (29th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Military operations in eastern Rehe seem to be imminent. It is rumored that the enemy will attack our positions on April 1st or 3rd. Our ××× division is on high alert. (29th Dispatch)

(Beiping) According to external sources, after withdrawing from the League of Nations, the Japanese are determined to actively expand the scope of their military operations. They will launch a general offensive on all passes of the Great Wall with their main force in Rehe. After occupying them, they will leave a considerable number of troops stationed there to prevent our counterattacks. Then, they will dispatch large numbers of troops from both Dulun and the coasts of Shandong to invade our North China provinces from the west, in order to achieve their ambition of completing a puppet Great Yuan state. However, our country is determined to resist, and the enemy will not succeed. (29th Dispatch)

(Beiping) A train of enemy armored vehicles was very active back and forth east of the Shi River railway bridge yesterday. Yesterday afternoon, more than 20 enemies searched and advanced towards our Shi River position and were repelled by our guards. Fierce fighting has been going on for days near Jiǔménkǒu. A certain unit of the enemy army in Yuguan has set off to provide support. The enemy near Jiǔménkǒu has been surrounded by our army. (29th Dispatch)

(Beiping) A telegram from Kaiping on the 28th stated that after being frustrated, the enemy did not attack again, but bombarded with artillery and aircraft every day. At night, we used various methods to harass the enemy. From 8:00 AM on the 27th, the enemy sent a large number of aircraft to bombard Jianchangying and nearby villages, including incendiary bombs, killing several villagers. Our positions were well-hidden and suffered very little damage. At noon, two enemy reconnaissance planes flew south to Qian'an for reconnaissance. From 5:00 AM on the 28th, both sides began artillery fire. (27th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Song Zheyuan telegraphed to Beiping that after the enemy in the direction of Luowenyu retreated to Kuancheng and Pingquan, only plainclothes teams were left on the front line, moving back and forth. Our army has partially advanced forward, and most are waiting for orders to advance. Furthermore, the enemy who retreated from the Great Wall has moved towards Fengning, and there is indeed fighting in Fengning. (29th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) In recent days, the Japanese army in Yuguan has gradually increased its troop strength. Aircraft frequently scout the Shi River and Changli areas, seemingly preparing to invade the interior. Today and tomorrow are the most critical times. Our army is also stepping up its defenses. As soon as the enemy comes, they will be completely annihilated. (29th China United News Agency Dispatch)

Since Japan has withdrawn from the League of Nations and is determined to expand the war, it is feared that follow-up troops will continue to invade. (29th Dispatch)

Food and furniture were all looted, and old men, women and children were all raped and defiled, and more than eighty people including Ma Yongle and Chang Chuan were shot and killed. One route is by the troops of the traitor Liu Guitang, attached to a certain brigade of Japanese bandits, moving south from Jingpeng. The other route is by two detachments of the traitor Zhang Haipeng, attached to some Japanese bandits, moving west from the Cone Mountain. On the 26th, urgent orders were sent to the mouth brigade to prepare to intercept in the Banjietang area, and to the brigade and brigade in the Daliutangzi area. Du Jian was instructed to lead his troops to build fortifications and maintain strict vigilance. Also, at 2:13 PM today, two enemy planes flew from the northeast direction. The anti-aircraft machine gun team was instructed to concentrate fire, but they did not dare to fly low. They only circled in the high sky and dropped more than a dozen bombs in three directions inside and outside the city, lasting about twenty minutes. They then flew away from the northeast direction. At present, it has been reported that eight civilian households and more than ten soldiers, and more than thirty horses have been killed inside the city. The exact number of deaths and injuries is currently being investigated. In addition to strictly ordering the troops to step up preparations for advancing and attacking, I am sending this telegram. There will be a great discussion at tomorrow's Central Standing Committee. The League of Nations Advisory Committee Met Yesterday 219

The American Representative From 21 Countries in Attendance Remained Silent Throughout

It Was Resolved That It Was Not Necessary to Respond to Japan's Withdrawal From the League

The Report on the Non-Recognition of the Puppet State Was Submitted to the Subcommittee for Study

The Opinions of Various Countries on the Arms Embargo Were Not Entirely Consistent

The Advisory Committee Adjourned Until After Easter

(Geneva) The Advisory Committee of the League of Nations, organized to monitor the Sino-Japanese dispute, has now read Japan's notice of withdrawal from the League of Nations and Secretary-General Drummond's reply. The Advisory Committee has not yet decided to issue a new statement criticizing Japan's views in the Japanese notification. However, the Committee intends to quickly study the various issues arising from the non-recognition of "Manchukuo." In addition, the representatives of the various countries in the Committee will also seek the opinions of their respective governments on the layer of prohibiting arms shipments to belligerent countries. (28th Havas Dispatch)

The various issues arising from the non-recognition of "Manchukuo" include "Manchukuo's" request to join the International Postal and Telegraph Union, and the status of local officials to consuls stationed in Manchuria.

(Geneva) The League of Nations Advisory Committee met at 5:30 PM tonight and adjourned at 7:15 PM. At the time of adjournment, the date of the next meeting had not been decided. However, it is unlikely that it will meet again before Easter. The Advisory Committee discussed the general situation arising from Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations, but decided that no reply was necessary. Irish Representative Lester first raised the issue of Japan's withdrawal, saying that he knew this matter was only indirectly related to the Advisory Committee, but he felt that the Advisory Committee might as well take a stand and respond to Japan's notice of withdrawal. The reply should point out that Japan has the right to know how to interpret international treaties regarding Japan's relations with other countries and should reject it. There was some discussion on this point among the members, but it was finally decided that since the Secretariat had already replied to the various sections in the Japanese document, the Advisory Committee did not need to reply. The Advisory Committee then listened to a report by the Deputy Secretary of the League of Nations, Mr. Pirrotti, on the issue of non-recognition of "Manchukuo." The report stated what actions should be taken regarding "Manchukuo's" request to join the Postal and Telegraph Alliance, and how the "Manchukuo" stamps, coins, passports, and other items should be treated. This report is not yet complete and will be submitted to the Subcommittee on the Non-Recognition of "Manchukuo." This committee will be convened after Easter. The Advisory Committee then discussed the issue of an arms embargo in order to prepare the agenda for the Arms Embargo Committee. However, the general opinion was that the attitude of a certain great power towards this matter was still uncertain, so there was nothing that could be done about it at present. It was felt that it would be better to wait and see the results of the proposed arms embargo related to the dispute with the two South American countries. Czech Representative Gisesti (Czech Minister to Switzerland) made a very clear statement, asking about the attitude of the United States towards this matter, but U.S. Representative Wilson was present as an observer and remained silent throughout, neither participating in the discussion nor expressing the views of his government, so the date of the Arms Embargo Committee meeting has not been set, but it will probably have to wait until after Easter. Only twenty-one countries, including the United States, attended today's meeting. The Turkish representative was not present. The British representative was External Secretary Kerr, France was represented by Massigli, and Germany was represented by Kenna. (28th Reuters Dispatch)

The U.S. Will Request Allocation

Territories Under Japanese Mandate 220

The Tokyo Hochi Shimbun reported on the 26th that, regarding the issue of the South Pacific mandated islands after Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations, the United States is extremely concerned due to their location and significant relationship to American naval operations in the Pacific. According to sources from Washington officials, the top leaders of the US government believe that Japan, having already withdrawn from the League of Nations, should not demand sovereignty over the mandated territories. If Japan stubbornly insists on its views, a serious protest will be lodged. The American position is that the mandated territories should be returned to the League of Nations. The territories acquired by the United States through the victory of the Allied Powers over the past decade or more were not individually ceded to the victorious nations but to the Allied Powers as a whole, and the United States naturally has a portion of the rights. Furthermore, the Secretary of State during President Wilson's era had already stated that the United States, as one of the main Allied nations, has the same concerns and inseparable interests in Germany's former overseas territories as other Allied nations. Therefore, other Allied nations also have an equal right to speak, and any disposal without the consent of the United States will be deemed invalid.

The Tokyo Nichinichi Shimbun reported that Germany will begin negotiations with Japanese Ambassador to Germany Nagai regarding the South Pacific mandated territories. The preliminary talks already took place at 8:00 PM on the 24th at a certain location in Berlin. Approximately twenty figures, including Nazi Party leader and Propaganda Minister Goebbels, Director of the Foreign Ministry's Information Department Frank, Acting Foreign Minister Rosenberg, and individuals involved in German foreign relations, secretly conferred with Acting Japanese Ambassador Fujii and others. As a result, the opinion put forward by the German side stated that Germany considers the South Pacific islands to have no current economic colonial value. However, fearing that the National Socialist Party might insist on reclaiming old colonies from the past, Germany recognizes that the South Pacific islands have important military significance for Japan. Therefore, Japan can practically utilize them militarily, but formally, they can be placed under German administration.

German Newspaper Criticizes

Japan Destroys League of Nations Organization 221

The Realization of East Asian Monroe Doctrine is Not Far Off

(Berlin) The nationalist "Berliner Börsen-Zeitung" commented on the issue of Japan and the League of Nations, believing that the League of Nations and the great powers are incapable in the Far East. Therefore, in the near future, Japan's attitude will not change in any way. The newspaper stated, "Japan's attitude will not change in any way. The newspaper stated that Japan has now withdrawn from the League of Nations, which shows that the League of Nations has no ability to maintain world peace, and Japan is unwilling to participate in the situation created by the Treaty of Versailles again. Since 1918, the Sino-Japanese issue has been the biggest dispute internationally. Since the League of Nations has no ability to resolve it, it will be impossible to make people value this kind of international organization and achieve the expected results in the future. Therefore, if the situation created by the Treaty of Versailles truly collapses and becomes a reality, we should regard Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations as the starting point of the League of Nations' bankruptcy." The newspaper also said, "The separation of Asia from Europe and the United States has long been a concern for the general public. Since Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations, this separation has been realized. In the future, Japan will declare the Far East as its own sphere of interest and will not allow interference from other countries. This policy will definitely be realized, the only unknown thing is when. Looking at Japan's attitude towards the former German islands in the Pacific, it can be seen that the time for Japan to adopt this policy may not be far away." The newspaper also believes that, apart from the United States, no other country can prevent Japan's progress. The newspaper concluded, "From our point of view, Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations can prove the League of Nations' incompetence on the one hand, and on the other hand, it can prove that only strong and resolute countries can defend themselves and survive in the daily struggles in the international arena. This is the greatest significance of Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations." (Havas dispatch on the 28th)

Second Japanese

Emigration Plan to the Northeast 224

Domei News Agency, Tokyo, 29th - The Japanese Ministry of Colonial Affairs, the Army Ministry, and the Kwantung Army Immigration Department have decided on the fundamental policy regarding the second armed immigration plan to Manchuria. This afternoon, the Ministry of Colonial Affairs invited representatives of demobilized soldiers to discuss the area for recruiting immigrants and the method of personnel allocation. As a result, it was decided that the immigration site this time will be near Yongfeng, Jiamusi, Jilin Province, which was the site of the first immigration last year. The qualifications for applicants are demobilized soldiers under the age of 30. Their selection will be determined by the local military headquarters and demobilized soldiers' associations. There will be a total of five hundred personnel. After one month of training at a field training center, they will be dispatched to the actual site.

Under German Government Guidance

Nationwide Anti-Jewish Movement Implemented 227

Strict Restrictions on Jewish Occupations

Jewish Shops Have Few Customers

Reuters, Berlin, 28th - The government today announced a widespread boycott of Jewish occupations, as retaliation for overseas Jewish plots against Germany. The German boycott is scheduled to begin at 10:00 AM on April 1st and will be rigorously implemented by boycott committees across the country. These committees will be responsible for monitoring and punishing offenders and for protecting the personal freedom of foreigners, regardless of their race or nationality. The boycott will be publicized to the public, and German families will not subscribe to newspapers that do not join the boycott. German stores are not allowed to advertise in these newspapers. The anti-Jewish boycott committee must also be responsible for investigating Germans who have deposits abroad and should use these funds to promote the truth that Germany is currently very peaceful domestically. The committee must strictly limit the number of Jews entering universities or holding medical and legal positions, so that their total number has a certain proportion to the total German population. The declaration states that the boycott should be implemented in a normal and peaceful manner and should not harm a hair on any Jew's head. The declaration fiercely criticizes the Jews, accusing them of believing in Marxism and blaming Germany for not banning immigrants in the past fifteen years, which led to a small number of Jewish writers, university professors, and businessmen repaying kindness with hatred and inciting the world against the Germans. Some towns in Germany have already started boycotting Jewish businesses. Stormtroopers from the National Defense Party have come out to order Jewish stores to close. Jewish lawyers and doctors in the Glöglau area have been forced to stop working. Customers are being prevented from entering Jewish-owned stores in the town of Gleiwitz in Upper Silesia, so although the stores are open, there is no business all day long.

Braunschweig, Germany

Discord Between Two Right-Wing Parties 241

Officials Believe it is a Local Incident

Insufficient to Affect Future Cooperation

Order Dissolving the Steel Helmet is Revoked Immediately

Reuters, Berlin, 28th - Today, official sources claimed that the discord that occurred a few days ago between the National Socialist Party and the Steel Helmet in Brunswick has been investigated, and it is known that this is purely a local incident. The cooperation between the National Socialist Party and the Steel Helmet in other parts of the country has not been affected by this. The leader of the Steel Helmet ridiculed the claim that the group was plotting to revolt against the government. It is expected that after the leaders of the Steel Helmet in Brunswick are replaced, the state's Minister of the Interior, Klagges, will withdraw the order dissolving the group.

Reuters, Berlin, 29th - The government today issued an order to lift the ban on the Steel Helmet, effective April 1st. At the same time, it praised the State Interior Minister of Brunswick, Klagges, for issuing the order to dissolve the Steel Helmet.

Havas, Berlin, 28th - The order dissolving the Steel Helmet party in Brunswick will be revoked on April 1st. Tonight, a delegation from the Federal Government, chaired by the leader of the Steel Helmet and Minister of Labor, Seldte, held a meeting with the Brunswick authorities in the state capital. After the meeting, the Prime Minister of Brunswick declared to the press that the harm caused by Marxists engaging in illegal activities under false pretenses no longer exists, so the order dissolving the Steel Helmet can be canceled. He also said that Mr. Seldte has agreed to resolve the matter in accordance with Steel Helmet discipline, and the central government has recognized the Brunswick's strict measures against the Steel Helmet as legitimate.

Reuters, Washington, 28th - Government personnel, including the army, navy, and air force, will be affected by the salary cuts, which will save a total of US$125 million annually. President Roosevelt stated in the order that the cost of living in the United States has fallen by 21.7% since 1992.

Promoting Afforestation to Reduce Unemployment 244

Havas, Washington, 28th - The House of Representatives passed a bill allowing the government to hire 250,000 unemployed workers to engage in afforestation.

Plans for Rural Relief Prepared 245

Havas, Washington, 28th - Agriculture Secretary Wallace submitted a plan to Congress to relieve farmers: (1) Farmers' debts will be submitted to arbitration for resolution with the consent of both creditors and debtors; (2) In order to facilitate indebted farmers, lending institutions will be established, and banks will lend small amounts to farmers for a maximum period of two years, so that farmers can use them to repay debts and pay taxes; (3) Allow the Federal Reserve Banks to issue Reconstruction Finance Corporation bonds to banks, transferring farmers' loans from the banks to the Federal Reserve Banks.

British Plane Crash 247

Fifteen Passengers Killed

Reuters, Dixmuide, 28th - The British passenger plane City of Liverpool crashed today in Humes, 20 miles north of here, between Brussels and Courtrai. All fifteen people on board, including the pilot and passengers, were killed. Among them were 11 British, 3 Germans, and 1 Belgian. About an hour after the plane took off from Haren Airport near Brussels, it suddenly caught fire and descended. None of the three pilots and twelve passengers survived. According to eyewitnesses, smoke was first seen coming from the plane, followed by a raging fire. The plane then spun downward and crashed after a short while, with a loud explosion. One person was seen jumping out of the plane. The plane crashed from a height of 300 yards. There were two dead bodies next to the plane, with broken limbs. The rest were all in the plane and burned to death. The site of the crash is now under guard, and no one is allowed to take pictures. The cause of the accident was investigated this afternoon and will continue tomorrow.

Japan Transports Cash to the United States 248

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 29th - The Japanese government bought 1,200 kan of gold bars, worth 11.2 million yen at market prices. The Kawasaki liner Ryoyo Maru, which departed from Kobe yesterday, is transporting them to San Francisco. This is the first shipment of gold bars this year to be sent to exchange banks to pay for overseas cash transfers without using bills of exchange. On the one hand, it aims to save overseas payments, and on the other hand, it encourages the gold production industry. However, as a result, there is a risk of increasing imports. At this time when the Exchange Control Law is in effect, it is extremely important to pay attention. According to observations from financial industry insiders, the government's transportation of cash is to prevent the exchange rate from falling and to gradually increase the US exchange rate to US$25, and then decisively implement a low parity.

Reuters Hollywood - A salary reduction movement for movie stars is currently underway, and the usually favorable contracts will also be revised. Stars who earn £1,600 per week and £50,000 per film, such as Greta Garbo, Norma Shearer, Myrna Loy, Swanson, the Marx Brothers, Ann Harding, William Powell, and George Arliss, will be greatly affected. Ann Harding may appear on the British stage. Norma Shearer plans to make one film each in England and France every autumn. Her contract stipulates that she will shoot four new films in two years, two films each year, and guarantees that her salary of £200 per day will not be affected in any way. It is quite difficult to know what Garbo's plans are. Arliss will return to England for recuperation, or will reappear on the stage, is yet to be decided. Swanson may organize her own independent film company or sign a contract with two or three major film companies. William Powell and Claudette Colbert will continue their screen careers, but they firmly oppose salary cuts. After the salary cuts, Powell's weekly income will be reduced to £1,600, and Colbert's will be reduced to £1,500.

All agencies affiliated with the Municipal Government, the City Party Headquarters, the Shanghai County Government, the Seafarers' Special Party Headquarters, the Garrison Headquarters, the Two-Road Special Party Headquarters, and the City Chamber of Commerce continued to operate as usual and held memorial meetings for the martyrs separately, as ordered.

(3) Recognize that the success of the Xinhai Revolution was due to the determination of the past ten revolutions, unity, and common commitment to national crisis. Then, our Northeast will be recovered one day, and the national humiliation can be avenged." The meeting did not end until 12:00 noon.

Song Ziwen Returns to Shanghai This Morning

It is Not a Problem for Dean Wang to Resume Office 255

The Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement Expires and is Abolished

Unification of Currency and Reorganization of Various Taxes

Song Ziwen, Vice President of the Executive Yuan, left Nanjing on the overnight express train last night and returned to Shanghai at approximately 8:00 AM this morning. Reporters from various newspapers called on Mr. Song at his private residence this morning. According to Mr. Song's statement, the issue of Wang Jingwei's return to the position of President of the Executive Yuan can be formally resumed after a decision is made by the Central Political Council this morning. The following is a record of Mr. Song's remarks:

Wang Will Immediately Resume Office 256

Mr. Song stated that there is absolutely no problem with Mr. Wang's return to the position of President of the Executive Yuan. He will formally resume his position after the Central Political Council resolves this issue this morning and will be fully responsible for politics thereafter. He himself will focus on finance. Therefore, what I can discuss with you gentlemen is limited to financial matters. Although I still hold the position of Vice President of the Executive Yuan, the Vice President does not have the authority to make statements related to the Executive Yuan.

Jiang to Come to Shanghai News 257

The reporter then inquired whether the news that Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, was about to come to Shanghai was accurate. Mr. Song did not give a definite answer, only saying that he had seen this item recorded in the newspapers, but he did not deny it either. It is said that Chiang will come to Shanghai within a day or two after attending today's Central Political Council meeting.

Unify Subsidiary Currency 258

Mr. Song also stated that various commercial organizations have requested the unification of subsidiary currency, and this matter can be done. In addition to copper and silver subsidiary currencies, our country currently does not have nickel coins. Nickel coins are more difficult to imitate. Most countries often use these nickel coins to transform armaments, such as bullet heads, etc., during emergencies, and the supply of raw materials is difficult. As for implementing the gold standard, it is also difficult because countries that implement the gold standard buy silver with gold, which is cheaper, while countries that do not use the gold standard find it extremely difficult to buy gold with silver. Whether the World Economic Conference will be held in May has not yet been decided, so it is not yet possible to predict whether I will go to Europe to attend.

Tariff Agreement 259

The Sino-Japanese tariff agreement will expire and become invalid after May 16. There is no question of whether it will be renewed, because the agreement only stipulates that the import tax on certain goods will be maintained for one and three years. Initially, because our country signed an agreement on tariff autonomy with various countries, Japan could not be an exception, so it maintained its minimum tariff rate, hence this provision.

Reorganize Tax Revenue 260

Regarding the reorganization of tax revenue, there is no problem in North China since it belongs to the central government, and there is also no problem in South China. Song explained that the "unification" of tax revenue does not mean that it is considered unified only if the central government sends people to handle tax collection. In general, anything that can be handled according to the methods of the central government is also called unified. Therefore, the central government strives to simplify the reorganization of tax revenue as much as possible. As for the reorganization of salt tax, the situation is also better now than before.

Borrowing RMB 100 Million It is said that the contract content is that the Sino-German joint venture steel plant will borrow a huge amount of US$25 million (one saying US$26 million) from Germany, calculated at 4 yuan per US dollar, reaching RMB 100 million, which is one of the largest amounts of foreign loans ever made by the government. British Malaya Peninsula

Strictly Limit Overseas Chinese Freedom to Land 268

Datong News Agency reported that the British Malaya Peninsula has always been free to land, so overseas Chinese who want to go to the island to engage in business can land freely without being bound by any conditions. However, recently, the British government authorities, in view of the fact that overseas Chinese residing in various places in Siam in Southeast Asia are unable to withstand the severe oppression of the governments of those places and have gone to the Malay Peninsula one after another to seek a living, which has greatly affected the power of British merchants in the area, recently promulgated twelve extremely harsh rules for overseas Chinese landing. All Chinese who wish to go to the island in the future must first fulfill the above-mentioned treaties, otherwise they will be forcibly sent back to their country of origin, and they will not be allowed to land freely. It is now known that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs believes that the British government's move is completely unreasonable, so it has lodged a protest with the British government, demanding that it immediately revoke the order restricting overseas Chinese from freely landing on the Malay Peninsula in order to enhance the friendship between the two countries.
