Talks

One Pass, Separated by Bitterness and Joy 272

— Wen Shan

Some days ago, newspapers reported that Mr. Wang Maosheng had secretly escaped from Shenyang to Shanghai. He actually dared to imitate the tongue of important people and published a piece of news, roughly saying that the Japanese rebels subjected the 30 million compatriots in Northeast China to various cruel punishments such as rape, looting, and murder, and confiscation of property, which was enough to darken the sky and the earth. However, they treated the captured soldiers of the Volunteer Army with even more "dismemberment by five horses" and the unheard-of "hanging upside down on treetops, causing their heart blood to flow downwards until death," a slow and torturous method of killing. In the world, there are no more inhumane things that defile the history of mankind than this.

In addition, the enemy army's severe and cruel punishments for our Northeast compatriots and the Volunteer Army, with their barbaric bestiality, are unimaginable. There must be more than just what Mr. Wang saw and heard and dictated. Perhaps there are even more severe and cruel things than what Mr. Wang dictated. I don't know how many. However, even with the particularly cruel torture of "hanging upside down on treetops," it is enough for us to make our hair stand on end, our eyes crack, and our hearts ache. Why do I say this? When we bravely fight for national personality and national freedom, we "cut with knives" instead of "shooting," nor do we use "burning" or "burying alive," but endure the slow and poisonous torture of hanging upside down on treetops, exposing them to the summer sun or autumn sun until their skin is scorched, or drifting in the wind and snow until their hearts are frozen. Yet their eyes are still shining, and their breath is still faint, unable to live and unable to die. The Japanese rebels standing under the tree and looking up are still clapping their hands and laughing. Alas, the cruelest things in the world can be said to end here!

The rich old men and young ladies who sing and dance and enjoy the southern scenery, the frontier drums have moved the earth. Please, when the singing and dancing stop, think about the soldiers of the Volunteer Army who are hanging upside down on treetops, put yourselves in their shoes. If you are not touched and do not think of any way to act spontaneously, then you are truly numb, living corpses whose hearts have already died!

Although, the country has reached today, and there are still such peaceful scenes to embellish it, it cannot be said that it is an intentional or unintentional revelation from those above. Please see, our respected gentlemen, are still leisurely and leisurely about the long-vacant central positions, and follow the way of the former kings, and give way to the country. You push me and I push you, and you are very polite! It is almost more than Yao and Shun giving way, and Chao and Xu avoiding far away. If it were not that they had truly planned a unified plan that was enough to win thousands of miles away on diplomacy, people were not made of wood and stone, and they were party and state dignitaries who were admired by tens of thousands of people, how could they be so well-prepared? Mr. Wang Maosheng, an ignorant refugee, has come to Shanghai. Why don't you be honest and have to learn to publish news? Don't be surprised that this kind of news material will offend those above. Even I, who am below, feel a deep unease when I hear it: the contradiction between the bitterness and joy of people, especially people of the same country, is becoming increasingly acute, which is not a good thing!

Science

Varnish 273

— Jiaxiang

As everyone knows, to make woodenware beautiful, just apply a kind of "varnish" (WoodVarnish) on the woodenware, and it can make the woodenware shine brightly. Ordinary varnish is only made by dissolving "shellac" in alcohol, or even mixing a part of rosin in shellac. This kind of impure varnish can only keep the shine for a short period of time when applied to woodenware. If varnish is prepared according to the following method, it can make the shine lasting and is very easy to dry. It can be used for high-end woodenware:

Raw Material Name　Mixing Amount

Shellac........................................4 ounces

Refined Camphor..........................1.43 ounces

Sandarach....................................4 ounces

Venice Turpentine.....................................1/2 ounce

(Venice Turpentine)

1 ounce

Methylated Spirit (Note).........................20 ounces

Mastic........................................1/2 ounce

Production method: Mix all the items on the right in a porcelain pot, then heat them until all kinds of things are completely dissolved in the methylated spirit and become liquid. Then take a fine gauze cloth, filter it, remove the dregs, and put it into a bottle, and the varnish is complete.

How to use: When varnish is stored in a bottle, the bottle stopper must be sealed to prevent air leakage. When using it, dip a soft brush or cotton cloth in the varnish and gently apply it on the woodenware. When applying it, it must be fast and orderly, and it must be even and smooth. If you want to renovate old woodenware that has been coated with varnish, then you only need to apply it directly. If you want to change the new woodenware to any color, you only need to dissolve any "aniline" dye in boiling water, first apply it on the wood, and then apply varnish after it dries. If you want to change it to the common orange-yellow color, then you only need to mix Bismarck brown into the varnish, and you can directly apply it on new woodenware.

Note: If methylated spirit is not available, pure alcohol can be used instead.

Literature and Art

Gold Trade 274

— Bai Jiao

Gold is exhausted, humans treated like dogs. Though prostrate, still capable of a lion's roar.

We look at each other and smile, like willows in the wind. Seeking high reputation for a thousand autumns.

Sucking blood, mouths wide open like whales. Coconut-sellers borrow to cover big hands.

Ascending to the sky in broad daylight, walking amidst the clouds. Speaking freely, unashamed of principles.

Skeletons once built human heroes. Who among the bandits ever carried a knife?

History only records thieves like Mao. Who pities the people as grubs in red mud?

Reading only reveals delicate beauties in books. Ten years under the window is truly in vain.

Old horses with blind eyes laugh at you all. Singing a wild song, pouring out fragrant wine.

Dove in Snow

Dove in snow, seeking sugary dregs. Guzzling, unable to fly.

Year after year, cold and heat cycle. One full meal, one hungry spell, all desiring death!

Draining ulcers, lancing hemorrhoids at the gates of noble lords. Shepherds driving away the pigs of Liaodong.

That day, the lad playing the flute in the Wu market. No one on the seat praises national heroes.

Entering the kennel, taming tigers like cats. Crossing the Huai, oranges all turn to trifles!

Fine silks and satins consume the energy of oxen. After wine, before flowers, discussing national shame.

Golden three burrows, gentle and plentiful. Returning home in silk, fiercely gazing around.

Slaying dragons as easily as slaughtering dogs. I just pass down straight as the sky (yet rewarded)...

Shop Employee Correspondence

Too Hard on My Daughter! 275

Editor:

I sent you a letter entitled "Such Parents" last time, and I am grateful that you published it in the newspaper on the 20th of this month. When I saw the response letter, thinking of the blood ties, I immediately went to the bank and withdrew the three hundred yuan I had saved from household expenses over the past six months to subsidize my family. Who knew that after receiving this three hundred yuan, they bought a large coat for each of my three younger brothers and two younger sisters, each costing over thirty yuan, and also bought leather shoes for over ten yuan a pair. Furthermore, they went to foreign barbershops to perm and wash their hair. It pains me so much that the household expenses I had painstakingly saved over half a year were all spent on decoration! Yesterday, my mother asked me to give them another one hundred yuan. Because they do not cherish my money, I refused her request, and she scolded me for being a miser and having no sisterly feelings at all. Sir, please tell me how should I treat this kind of biased mother? With respect, Jiang Shimeiying

××××

Editor's Note: After reading Mrs. Jiang's latest letter, we now know that her parents are indeed too hopeless: no wonder their daughter is unwilling to subsidize them! We dare not advise Mrs. Jiang to spend her husband's hard-earned money so carelessly. Because this could cause her parents to fall further and further down; and it could also turn her younger siblings into vagrants who "only know how to squander and do not know the cost of things."

Blood ties still exist; Mrs. Jiang must put in more effort. Your parents are getting older, so that is not a problem. But your younger siblings are still young, and you must not only refrain from watching them starve to death without helping, but you should also actively take responsibility for their education. In the future, if they succeed, it will also be to your credit; and it will also create some talents for China, or at least reduce the number of free riders for the country.

Therefore, we advocate that Mrs. Jiang should not unconditionally subsidize her family in the future; you should be responsible for your younger siblings' education expenses, and you may directly pay the school fees. You should also check their schoolwork at any time. As for daily necessities, buy some to give to them when they are truly needed. As for your mother's harsh words, you do not need to take them to heart, as everyone around you can see who is right and who is wrong!

Fiction

Time in a Dream (Continuation 15) 276

— Qin Shouou

"No! Absolutely not! I can swear there isn't!" Wu Yi vigorously knocked a clothes brush on a wooden frame holding a sand water filter. "If you say the Kuomintang is the Republic of China, then their party anthem is of course the national anthem! But I'm the first not to acknowledge it!"

"Old Roar, calm down, discussing the main matter is important!" Ma Liguo hurriedly shifted the conversation to the main topic. "Because just now the ship owner discussed with me: he said that a distinguished guest came aboard after passing Honolulu, that is our National Government's plenipotentiary minister to the United States, Dr. Liu. In order to show the emotional bond between Chinese and American people, they plan to have their band play a Chinese national anthem during dinner tonight. But they don't have the score there, so they asked me to write it out for them. Suppose, ... suppose your words are true, wouldn't this be terrible? How can we say that China has no national anthem!"

"Ah! ... Haha! So that's what it's all about. But what if China really doesn't have a national anthem?" Wu Yi replied, both angry and amused.

"Really doesn't have one?" Ma Liguo still couldn't fully believe it.

"Really doesn't have one! Most likely, the government, because the national treasury is empty, so it has no power to write one!" Apart from this "misinterpretation", even if you brought old Master Yan Pingzhong, who was good with words, out of his coffin, I'm afraid you wouldn't be able to find another sufficient reason to explain why the Great Republic of China has no national anthem!

"In that case, you, my old friend, are a great author, so please make one temporarily!" Ma Liguo truly deserves to be the son of an important Chinese figure. He is extremely familiar with the set of tricks in Chinese politics, where every time there is a change, people are randomly pulled from within the party to serve as ministers in various departments. He thought that as long as someone had a slight skill, they would be an omnipotent treasure: someone who had been a military commander could concurrently serve as a diplomat; someone who had been a university president might as well be transferred to head the Ministry of Communications. Therefore, he also thought that since Wu Yi was an author, he would certainly be able to fill in a song score!

"Isn't this a joke! Not to mention that I don't understand music and can't fill it in, even if I could, a national anthem can't be fabricated casually! I remember that before the Kuomintang came into power and before the three northeastern provinces were lost, we did have a very magnificent national anthem, the one that goes 'Qing Yun Chou Xi...' But now, it's not allowed, if you sing another sentence, you can't escape the crime of being a counter-revolutionary, and maybe there's even hope of being shot! ... Haha! ... "Wu Yi ridiculed in an extremely painful tone. "However, if they really want to play it, you can directly ask Minister Liu himself. See what he orders?"

"That's right! That's right!" Ma Liguo was overjoyed to be able to approach Minister Liu through this, and he really went.

He was gone for a full forty minutes before he returned, his attitude very excited, holding a letter in his hand neatly. "Your words are true! Minister Liu also said that our national anthem has not yet been produced; but he has already thought of a compromise, he personally wrote this letter, teaching me to hand it over to the captain. Look!"

Wu Yi indeed pulled out two pages of letter paper from the envelope. Looking at it, the first page was a very beautiful English letter. The general idea was: "The score of the Chinese national anthem is extremely complicated, and it is really difficult to copy out temporarily; but since you have shown great hospitality and plan to play our national music to show your welcome to my humble person, then I dare not disappoint you too much. I am specially recording an ancient song of our country, which at that time described the spirit of envoys going abroad to foreign countries and never surrendering until death..." The second page was the sheet music for "Su Wu Herding Sheep."

"What a good compromise! Truly worthy of being an old diplomat!" Wu Yi praised with great satisfaction, "Otherwise, Chinese people without a national anthem really wouldn't know how to cover their shame!"

Interview with the Captain of the Wufa Photographic Expedition (Part 1) 277

— Xin Fu

On the third day after Dr. Ulrich K.T. Schulz, the leader of the Wufa Photographic Expedition, returned to Berlin from Northern Europe, a reporter went to the Wufa Company to interview him. Stepping into the doctor's office, it looked very much like a scientist's or explorer's laboratory. They started talking unceremoniously in such a place:

"You want to see me? Good, then please tell me what you want to ask!"

"Please tell me, what were you thinking about before I came in?"

"Think! I, who left Berlin for five months and just returned from working in Northern Europe: apart from the films taken in Northern Europe and the local customs, what else would I be thinking about? Believe me, the things in the North are all different from here. I had the idea of "going to Northern Europe" a long time ago, but my courage was repeatedly thwarted by the severe cold weather in Northern Europe, but now I have finally achieved my goal. This time, thanks to the excellent equipment, we took many valuable films. We not only captured scenes on and under the water: but also drove airplanes to capture them in the air. Ten thousand five thousand feet high is not a matter. The mouth of the Norwegian fjord is two hundred and sixty miles across the continent. In addition to flying across, we also sat on sailboats, back and forth among the cliffs.

Taking the scene of fish schools spawning in still water."

"Would you like to tell me about your most interesting experience this time?"

"I'm very willing. On the shore of the fjord, there are many trees with flowers in full bloom. Imagine such beautiful trees, with cliffs and white snow on their backs, and a vast ocean in front of them. What an interesting natural beauty! Therefore, when we flew across the fjord, we used reflective photography to capture many wonders."

"What is reflective photography? Could you explain it to me?"

"Ordinary photography is opposite to sunlight. This is a good way to let the object receive sunlight and reflect light; but our photography is against sunlight. This method has not been invented for long, it is not only convenient, and the wonders that could not be captured before can now be captured: the beautiful scenery of the rapids and waterfalls that we captured this time are all using this method. (To be continued)

Audience Opinions

Several Submissions Regarding "Morning in the Metropolis" 278

(1) It is a Great Success 279

— Yan Jiling

In terms of consciousness, it also achieved great success. It does not have the petty bourgeois illusion of disillusionment, it indicates a bright future for the masses. It tells the suffering masses: don't be afraid of anything, don't accept the hypocritical pity of the rich, and don't covet personal enjoyment: only by struggling hard under the life of hardship and oppression, daring to give the oppressors a merciless and cruel beating, is the way out for the suffering masses.

In terms of performance, Gao Zhanfei and Wang Renmei are both very powerful. Yuan Congmei's villain is indeed an old hand. Tang Huaiqiu was too rigid when he first appeared, but later he was not bad. The rest, such as Wang Guilin and Liu Jiqun, are all very good. Yan Duoyun, who plays the young Xu Languang, has a lot of performing talent and is a promising child.

(2) He Also Says the Plot is Great 280

— Feng Ying

The true meaning of the script is worthy of our admiration. It shows the sacredness and nobility of labor everywhere. However, in a deformed society like China, not only is the class gap between rich and poor huge, but the social economy is also too unevenly distributed, resulting in the sacred and noble workers earning only enough to barely maintain their personal lives each day, while those capitalists who do not engage in production live a comfortable life without working. "Morning in the Metropolis" is a powerful cry for the sacred and noble workers of the masses, and at the same time, it undoubtedly gives the people of the times a great inspiration.

As for the actors, Gao Zhanfei's tough and profound performance made me feel infinite sympathy. Wang Renmei's innocence and brilliance made me feel that she was extremely lovable. Wang Guilin's loving father and son simply brought people to tears.

In short, this film has achieved great success in terms of performance and significance. However, in terms of plot, it seems a bit lacking in compactness.

"Ten Thousand Flowers Offering Charm" is a hot song and dance blockbuster starring Eddie Conte, which will premiere today at the Guanglu Lanxin Theater.

(3) But There Are Contradictions and Shortcomings 281

— Wan

The people immersed in the dark city are extremely depressed! Who doesn't dream of a ray of dawn coming to light our way to the light? Therefore, "Morning in the Metropolis" appeared in response to the needs of the times. It and "City Night" are films that are connected in one breath; the plot, performance, photography, everything, has the same tune played in different ways. However, the power of "City Night" is still a bit deeper! This film can also be regarded as a successful work by Lianhua. But looking closely, there are still many loopholes inside.

First, many actors don't know how to walk. Moving too fast shows that they are too hurried.

Second, when the workers pull the carts, they don't use any force at all, which clearly shows that they are filming a play.

Third, the part where the little Sanzi in the countryside is joking is a bit too much.

These are the shortcomings of the performance; there are also contradictions and ambiguities in the plot.

Mao Dun's Novel "Midnight" Will Be Filmed 282

— Zhao Peng

Hong Shen and Tian Han Suggest

Lianhua Company Adopts

The recent long novel "Midnight I" by the literary writer Shen Congwen (Mao Dun) depicts deeply and has profound implications, which has been warmly welcomed by people from all walks of life. Giants in the film and theater industry, Hong Shen, Tian Han, etc., specially suggested to Lianhua Company, advocating that Shen's long novel "Midnight" be adapted into a movie script, which has already been agreed by Cai Chusheng, the director of Lianhua Company. However, in order to maintain the true face of his work, Shen specially requested the authorities that the compilation of the script should not change the author's original intention, and the leading actors must be those who have cultivated in drama and literature; the author will personally direct the psychological descriptions so as to be meticulous. The company authorities deeply appreciated his intention and are now planning everything. As soon as everything is ready, filming will begin.

(4) A Few Words of Praise for Gao and Yuan 283

— Shen Qianli

I have learned a lot about the films starring Gao Zhanfei. However, there are not many that are satisfactory. "Pink Dreams" and "Dawn", which premiered not long ago, are considered by some people to be his success; but I think that he has only just entered the hall and has not yet entered the room. After "Morning in the Metropolis" was released, it told us that he has risen to the level of art and has seen the hall. Here he is impeccable. However, at the same time, I discovered that the script gave him a lot of help in this success. Otherwise, even if he has the talent for performance, it would be like "a hero with no place to use his strength."

I don't need to talk about Yuan Congmei, just borrow Cai Chusheng's words once; "...In his pure life, sin is impossible to break into, but due to his imagination and creation, he has in fact created his unique villain star status on the screen. ...And thank him for adding a lot of strength to "Morning in the Metropolis" in the opposite direction." Indeed, imagination and creation are indispensable elements for the success of every star, not only Yuan Congmei personally should do so.

(5) The Year Should Be Noted 284

— Huang Yingdai

The material of the whole play is completely implying the toxicity of inheritance to people, and the sacredness of labor makes the audience under the screen realize the true meaning of life. Of course, the result and effect are different from those scripts that are aimless and deliberately mischievous. We naturally have to say that this script is a success!

In terms of actors, the talents are very average, and there are few mistakes. What we especially admire is Wang Renmei's Lan'er. Her lively and innocent situation is just right for a village girl's identity. We hope that the directors of Lianhua can grasp her personality so that she can develop her acting talent.

However, from my subjective point of view, in "Morning in the Metropolis", the prologue of the whole play feels a little loose and cannot reach a very tense situation. As for the year indicating the progress of time, I think Chinese films should use the Republic of China × year instead of using subtitles such as 1919 丨 丨 1933, because we China also has its own inherent year number, so why borrow the Western calendar? I wonder what the readers think?

Huang Naishuang Founded a Song and Dance Research Group 285

Huang Naishuang, who plays the female lead in the happy film company's second production "Desperate", originally served as a basic actor in the Jinan Company. Huang also plays the lead role in the recent production "Striving for National Glory". Now that both films are about to be completed, I want to found a song and dance troupe in my spare time. Now I hear that I am already recruiting group members and have named it the Naishuang Song and Dance Research Group. Therefore, I think that in the near future, I may be able to meet them on stage!

One Five-Mile Plan" Fails 286

— Yun Jun

Recently, a strange event occurred in Old Hollywood Country, that is, the "Five-Mile Plan" of George Arliss, an English veteran star who is about to turn 65, that is, he has to walk five miles every morning.

On Cahuenga Road, the old and strong Mr. Arliss strode forward step by step. His car and his chauffeur followed behind.

When Mr. Arliss felt a little struggling to walk, he automatically walked to the car and jumped into the car. As a result, the so-called five-mile walk only walked one-fifth of the way, and the remaining four miles were carried by Arliss' car. The heart is more than enough but the strength is not enough, so the sensational "Five-Mile Plan" was declared a failure.

A Record of the Production Process of "Cavalcade" 287

— Lin

The American Fox Company's new mega-film named Cavalcade, the original book is written by the famous British novelist Noel Coward. The British Isles have been recited for a while and regarded as a masterpiece of national glory. The American Fox Company purchased the film production rights from the author for a huge sum of money and added a lot of energy to the production. British national public opinion was in an uproar, pointing out that Old Howard's move was a humiliation to the country. Now the Fox Company has spent millions of dollars to complete the filming of this film. Both sides of the Atlantic are sensationalized by it, and the greatness of its value can be imagined. It is planned to excerpt and enrich the film publication of this drama's story. However, there are still many anecdotes left behind before the filming of this film, which have not been told, so I will focus on describing them here as a guide to the translation.

The general idea of this book is to describe the tragic war suffered by Britain since the beginning of the 20th century and the pain of the disintegration and separation of a giant official's (the protagonist in the book) family, and to compare it with the peaceful scene of the Victorian era at the end of the 19th century, in which there are many emotionally moving places. The author sold the photography rights to Hollywood not to seek a large profit. Now that Fox Company has made the film, the author's heart can be reported to the British people without shame. The great financial resources used to produce this film almost relocated all the famous attractions of London in 1900 to Hollywood, so that the veterans who traveled there were almost suspicious of the former capital 30 years ago, and often felt grief and could not make a sound, which shows the precision and greatness of the arrangement.

After the photography rights of this book were sold to Hollywood by Coward and aroused the reaction of the British people, the Fox Company decided to use all British actors in the whole play in order to please the British and not lose the British nature. All those who were not born in London and educated in London were not allowed to be actors. Even directors, photographers, lighting engineers, etc. are all staffed by British people. Because of this, Fox heroines such as Ann Harding, Irene Dunne, and Irene Sheridan were not selected, and Diana Wynyard, who had just come to the United States from England, was used instead. Fox's famous director Paul Tschi can only participate in the work of preparation and production, and the real director is Frank Lloyd, a clever Englishman. Reginald Berkoy, a member of the British House of Commons, was also appointed as the film script editor.

Since the entire staff for the production and performance must be staffed by British people, the Fox Company felt the lack of British talent in the United States. Therefore, they had no choice but to send a special envoy to London to look for actors among the dancers and actors of the play. After several careful selections, they obtained several male and female actors. However, there were also difficulties in the middle, which were unexpected by the company. For example, the child actors in the play had already obtained considerable talents, and the contract had also been signed. Unexpectedly, when boarding the ship to the United States, they were suddenly banned by the British immigration authorities, because according to British law, there is a clause that "children under the age of fourteen shall not go abroad to perform for profit." The company was hindered by this, so they had to change their plans and look for roles in British families in the United States. (To be continued)
